Current Commentary

Anglo-Dutch Secret Agreement and British Naval Conference

Ever since Japan seized Manchuria and actively prepared for war, peace in the Far East has been on the verge of danger. Recently, it has held a puppet regime in place to claim an emperor and has tried to carry out a monopolistic policy in the Far East market. Not only have the United States and the Soviet Union been concerned about this, but also the interests of Britain, France, Italy, and the Netherlands in the Far East have been affected. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini expressed the "Yellow Peril" theory earlier, and former French Prime Minister Herriot discussed the Far East crisis with concern later. Today's Singapore Imperial Naval Military Conference, convened by Britain, is regarded by the Japanese as a dark cloud over the Pacific. It can be seen that various countries are urgently rising up to deal with Japan's monopolistic policy. The situation of tit-for-tat is already obvious. As for the Netherlands, as a small European country, it has always attached importance to colonial interests, especially the natural resources of the East Indies in the Pacific as the core of its national power. Therefore, its vigilance against Japan's ambitions is always present. According to a previous Lianhe News Agency telegram, the Japanese Consul in Chicago, Mutō, telegraphed the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating that a certain newspaper in Chicago had published that the Netherlands had established a secret naval agreement with Britain due to its relationship with the East Indies territory. The editorial also stated, "The dangerous object of the Dutch East Indies is Japan. The reason is the Borneo oil issue, which may cause disputes. Therefore, the Netherlands wants to place it under the protection of the British Navy." From this speculation, although nothing is known about the content of the agreement, it is highly possible that the Netherlands will unite with the British for the sake of safeguarding its interests. In terms of the economic status of the Dutch East Indies and its relationship with Japan, it is also closely related to the future of peace in the Far East.

The so-called Dutch East Indies usually includes Java, Sumatra, Dutch Borneo, Sulawesi, and other numerous islands. The total area is about 740,000 square miles, which is about seven times that of the Philippine Islands and fourteen times that of the British Malay Peninsula. It has a population of over 60 million, while the Philippines has only 13 million and the Malay Peninsula has less than 5 million. It is located southwest of the Philippines, between the Pacific and Indian Oceans. The wealth of resources, such as rubber, sugar, tea, coal, tin, and oil, is all available. Japanese immigrants and investments in the area have been around for a long time, and it has almost become the center of Japanese economic power in Southeast Asia today.

Secondly, Japan's trade relations in the East Indies are also in an absolutely advantageous position. In 1932, Japan's imports from the East Indies totaled 100 million yen, which is higher than that of the Netherlands, Britain, Germany, and the United States. In the same year, Japan's total exports from the East Indies were only 40 million yen. It can be seen that Japanese goods in the East Indies market are quite sufficient to overwhelm Britain, the Netherlands, and other countries and occupy a surplus position.

Thirdly, Dutch Borneo produces approximately 5 million metric tons of oil annually, which is one-twentieth of the total annual production in the United States. It is the most important oil source in Asia after Persia. Japan has always been an oil-importing country, and more than half of its oil is supplied by the East Indies. In the eleven months of 1933, the national oil imports with a specific gravity below 0.8762 were approximately 120 million gallons, of which 60 million gallons were imported from the East Indies. The national oil imports with a specific gravity below 0.73 were approximately 730,000 gallons, of which 670,000 gallons were imported from the East Indies. This is enough to show the extent of the importance of the Borneo oil mine to Japan's economy and national defense.

From the above, Japan has already gained a very close relationship with the economic status of the Dutch East Indies. If the Japanese once engage in economic aggression in Southeast Asia and do not hesitate to cause serious conflicts with the Far East interests of the British, then how dangerous will Britain be? Britain has been threatened by this major threat to its naval position in the Far East. Naturally, it must join hands with the Netherlands. With common interests, they must be close to each other. This is the natural trend.

Although the Japanese warlords are trying their best to realize the Asian Monroe Doctrine, they are only provoking the ill will of other countries. British territories have been stimulated by Japanese economic aggression so much that they have no choice but to devise a naval defense plan. Therefore, although the details of the Singapore Naval Conference are not yet clear, it can be predicted that there will be a strict arrangement to deal with Japan. On the one hand, it uses its diplomatic means to contact the Netherlands. Military strategy and diplomacy go hand in hand. It can be said that it has done everything possible to deal with Japan with meticulous planning. Is this why the Japanese feel the dimness of the Pacific war clouds and are frightened and uneasy?

The Sun-Ma Conflict Escalates

Both Sides Telegraph, Claiming Oppression

Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai Provinces Implement Joint Defense

Sun Dianying Actively Expands Troops

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan, concerned about the conflict between the Sun and Ma armies, intends to mediate. Wang Shiping visited Huang today afternoon, reporting on the conflict between the Sun and Ma armies. This evening, the 41st Army office received a telegram from Sun at the front, reporting that the Ma army has been actively oppressing for days, and the war has gradually escalated. The North China authorities have repeatedly received telegrams from Ningxia, stating that the Sun army's siege of Pingluo is very urgent, and that the Sun army's westward advance aims to pass through Ningxia to Shaanxi. Zhu Shaoliang has telegraphed Ping for days, expressing concrete opinions on resolving the Sun-Ma incident. The Ping authorities received an urgent telegram from Ma today, reporting that the Sun army's attack on Pingluo is fierce. Tianjin received a telegram from Sun, expressing being oppressed and reaching the point of final tolerance. The Gansu army Ma Bufang's division has arrived in Ningxia, and Hu Zongnan's division is concentrated in Lanzhou. The military of a certain Ningxia, Qinghai, and Gansu province has implemented joint defense. A major war in the Northwest is imminent. How to deal with it? He's response awaits Chiang's telegram decision. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) The North China military authorities and the central government have decided that the Sun troops should remain stationed in the Wuyuan, Suiyuan, and Linhe areas until the weather warms up, then a new relocation site will be determined. It is said that the issue will be discussed at tomorrow's Military Affairs Commission's routine meeting. He Yingqin will telegraph Sun tonight, instructing the troops to stop advancing westward and await orders. Hou Cheng's visit to Shanxi to discuss with Yan is also based on this point. Yan has already dissuaded Sun from advancing westward based on this intention. However, it is still difficult to predict whether Sun will stop military action as a result. According to a telegram from Ningxia, the Sun army cavalry is surrounding Pingluo County, and its infantry still intends to bypass Pingcheng and advance westward. The Ningxia provincial army, in order to protect the territory and secure the people, will cooperate to block the attack. Since Sun incorporated the bandits of Yang Xiaohou and Wang Ying, he has expanded the troop numbers greatly. Currently, Sun's troops include four infantry divisions: the 127th, 118th, and 119th divisions, each with three brigades, each brigade with three regiments; the 120th division with two regiments and one special service regiment; and a supplementary brigade, three cavalry divisions, each with three regiments; and three cavalry brigades, each with two regiments, as well as one artillery regiment, three battalions each of engineering and supply, and two battalions of military police, totaling more than thirty regiments. Only seven regiments of Sun's troops have been registered with the Military Affairs Commission, with a monthly budget of 220,000 yuan. Now it has increased a lot. The Military Affairs Commission will discuss the issue of Sun's expanded troops tomorrow. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Ma Hongbin and Ma Hongkui telegraphed Ping twenty times, stating that the enemy attacking Pingluo launched a fierce attack from all sides with artillery fire at midnight on the 20th. On the 21st, at dawn, the enemy infantry was extremely fierce, charging to the base of the city and climbing the city walls at great risk. The officers and soldiers of our Second Brigade bravely resisted, and after a fierce battle until noon, they were finally repelled. The enemy cavalry suffered too many casualties and appeared to be fleeing in panic. From the north of Pingluo City to Huangge, since the enemy surrounded the city, the enemy artillery has been constantly concentrating its bombardment. Our defending soldiers are doing their best to hold on, and are still in a stalemate. According to Zhang Chengde, an enemy artillery soldier captured, the enemy's main force has concentrated in the area north of Pingluo City, with twelve 36-style long-barreled guns, four mountain guns, and twelve heavy mortars. Sun Dianying and Liu Yueting are both in Huangquqiao, etc. (23rd Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) Hou Cheng, representative of the Ping Military Affairs Commission, received a telegram from He, instructing him to stay in Taiyuan for a while, pending the resolution of the Sun-Ma affair. Wang Jingguo is scheduled to visit Yan on the 32nd to report on the recent situation of defense after the departure of the Sun troops in western Suiyuan. (23rd Dispatch)

(Nanjing) A senior staff officer said that the war between the Sun and Ma armies has not stopped, and the two armies are still in a stalemate between Pingluo, Shizuishan, and Ningyuan. If the Ma troops lose Pingluo, then Ningxia will not be secure, so the two armies are fighting fiercely here. Although the central government has sent telegrams strictly ordering both sides to stop military action, the Sun troops, with their motley crowd of 60,000, disregard everything and continue to advance westward. The General Staff of the Military Affairs Commission is drafting a plan to deal with the situation, which will be submitted to Chairman Chiang for approval on the 23rd. (23rd Dispatch)

Song Zheyuan Will Return to Chahar

(Beiping) Song is scheduled to return to Chahar on the 3rd or 4th. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Regarding the Chahar Incident, the commander of the Japanese 8th Division, Nishi Yoshiichi, telegraphed military attache Chiba Yama, stating that our 29th Army is increasing troops to eastern Chahar. Chiba visited He yesterday to inquire. This morning, Song and Qin Dechun visited He to report that no troops have been added. Song will submit a report at tomorrow's Military Affairs Commission's routine meeting, and then determine a method to respond to the Japanese side. (23rd Dispatch)

President Wang Hosts a Banquet for Military and Political Leaders

(Nanjing) President of the Executive Yuan Wang Zhaoming hosted a banquet at his official residence on the 23rd for Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission Chiang Kai-shek, Central Committee member Zhang Xueliang, Standing Committee member of the Economic Council Song Ziwen, Secretary-General of the Central Committee Ye Chucang, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, Mayor of Shanghai Wu Tiecheng, Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo, Chief of Training Zhu Peide, President of the Military Advisory Council Tang Shengzhi, Chairman of Hubei Province Zhang Qun, Chairman of Henan Province Liu Zhi, Chairman of Fujian Province Chen Yi, Commander of the 32nd Army Shang Zhen, and Wang Shuchang, among others, more than ten people. During the event, they expressed their opinions on the political situation. The event ended happily at 10 p.m. (23rd Dispatch)

Xia Ziming Leaves Beiping to Return to Defend

(Beiping) Xia Ziming, commander of the Second Brigade of Chahar Province, returned to Huaian this afternoon to defend his post. Song sent Lü Xiuwen to accompany him to verify the situation. (23rd Dispatch)

Southwest Elects to Telegraph Fujian, Urging Li, Chen, and Chiang to Awaken and Resign

Chiang Guangnai Telegrams Guangdong to Discuss the Future of the 19th Route Army

(Hong Kong) Chiang Guangnai telegraphed Weng Guiyuan on the 22nd to discuss the future of the 19th Route Army. Weng forwarded it to the Political Council for discussion on the 23rd. (23rd Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Zhang Ruigui arrived in Hong Kong from Shantou on the 23rd. (23rd Dispatch)

Gu Weijun Tells German Reporters That the Japanese Army's Ambition is to Gradually Seize Eastern Mongolia

Our Country Persists in the Doctrine of Non-Recognition, and the Situation Between Japan and Russia Remains Very Tense

(Berlin) Today, Gu Weijun, the Chinese representative to the League of Nations, met with the Geneva correspondent of the Berliner Tageblatt and stated that China would adhere to its position of non-recognition regarding the situation created by Japan in the Far East. Mr. Gu pointed out that Japan's recent military actions, with its troops gradually expanding the area they occupy, have the clear purpose of annexing eastern Mongolia into the puppet state. The speed with which this plan is achieved depends on how Japan's relations with Soviet Russia develop. Although there have been reports of a gradual easing between the two countries recently, it is questionable whether this is simply the calm before a major storm. As for the puppet Puyi's claim to the throne, it has little practical effect, as Japan's ruling power remains unchanged. Mr. Gu also spoke of the good feelings between China and Germany, such as Germany's relinquishment of consular jurisdiction, which not only does not harm the safety of the German people, but has certainly increased the friendship between the peoples of the two countries. This can be seen in the fact that German goods sell well in China and that the Chinese government employs many German advisors. (22nd National Telegram)

British Cotton Industry Area Holds a Large Demonstration Against Japanese Goods Dumping

Demanding That the Government Abolish Preferential Treatment for Japan

Manchester Chamber of Commerce Offers Friendly Advice to Japan

(London) Manchester will hold a large demonstration against the dumping of foreign goods tomorrow. Representatives from all parts of the cotton goods industry and mayors from the most important cities in Lancashire will participate. The public will focus on Japanese competition and will discuss a resolution asking the government to abolish all most-favored-nation treatment treaties between Britain and Japan, and to use its influence to persuade the dominions and colonies to do the same. It is also planned to ask the government to enact laws prohibiting (1) the export of old British machinery, (2) the employment of foreign students in British factories, (3) British investment in Japanese industry, and (4) the misappropriation of British trademarks. (22nd Reuters Telegram)

(London) The annual report of the Manchester Chamber of Commerce contained friendly advice to Japan. The report acknowledged that the hard-working and enlightened Japanese people had a legitimate desire to advance their country, and continued that if the Japanese proceeded in an orderly and gradual manner, without creating an intolerable situation for other countries, their prosperity would be more stable and lasting than if they hastily disrupted the established patterns of world trade. The final result might be a solution that strengthens the world economy and contributes to the peaceful progress of all countries. The report also stated that the board of directors of the Chamber of Commerce felt that this matter involved the interests of the British people to a great extent and could no longer afford to waste time and wait for Japan's response. Therefore, representatives of the Chamber of Commerce are now preparing to begin active negotiations as soon as possible. If the current situation continues, the only way to solve the problem mutually is for Japan to adopt a plan to limit the quantity of its exports and set prices similar to those of Western products, otherwise the domestic and colonial markets within the British Empire will have to protect themselves with tariffs, quotas, or prohibitions, and other countries in the same situation will do the same. (22nd Reuters Telegram)

Sino-US Cotton and Wheat Loan Agreement to Be Amended Soon

It is Not Easy for Our Country to Promote American Cotton

(Washington) Today, Jesse Jones, director of the US Reconstruction Finance Corporation (RFC), announced that the Chinese government could not purchase $40 million worth of American cotton as agreed, so the two sides are now discussing reducing China's $50 million cotton and wheat loan. Jones also said that this loan was signed by Chinese Finance Minister Song Ziwen when he came to Washington, with $40 million for purchasing American cotton and $10 million for purchasing American wheat. However, to date, the Chinese government has only purchased $7 million worth of American cotton, and it is feared that the Chinese government will not be able to purchase the full $40 million worth of American cotton by the expiration date of the loan on July 1 this year. As for the $10 million wheat loan, Jones believes that it can be done, as the Chinese government seems to find it easier to promote American wheat than American cotton. How much the loan amount will be reduced is still under discussion, but Jones declined to say whether this move was initiated by the Chinese government. According to a recent Associated Press dispatch from Shanghai, the Chinese government does intend to amend the loan agreement. Jones also said that the RFC intends to limit its assistance to foreign countries in purchasing American goods in the future, as the RFC should not be lending to foreign countries at all. (22nd National Telegram)

France Restricts Our Country's Soybeans

(Paris) According to a government gazette, the import quota for Chinese soybeans is now set at 70,000 "Kantō" (one Kantō equals 100 kilograms), and the issuance of individual import licenses has been temporarily suspended. (23rd Havas Telegram)

The Japanese Parliament Reopens

Saitō Announces Administrative Policy, Hirota Delivers Foreign Policy Speech

Protecting the Puppet Manchuria, Inducing Friendship with China

Extravagant Talk of Peace with Russia, Easing Feelings with America

(Tokyo) The parliament, after its recess, convened at 10 a.m. on the morning of the 1st. First, Prime Minister Saitō delivered a policy speech in the Upper House, lasting about 20 minutes, followed by Foreign Minister Hirota's foreign policy speech, also lasting about 20 minutes. Then, Count Niara, of the Research Association, began a sharp interrogation on the issue of ideology, taking the first shot in the questioning war. The Lower House convened at 1 p.m. After Saitō and Hirota delivered the same speeches, Finance Minister Takahashi followed with a speech on financial policy. Mr. Tokonami Takejirō of the Seiyukai party fired the first arrow of questioning, followed by Mr. Machida Chuji of the Minseitō party. The leaders of the two parties, who had been silent for years, began a sharp questioning war. (23rd Dentsu Telegram)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota delivered a speech on foreign policy in the House of Peers at 11 a.m. today. The full text is as follows:

The Japanese government and the League of Nations have unfortunately held greatly differing opinions regarding the Manchurian Incident, the issue of "Manchukuo," and the fundamental significance of maintaining peace in East Asia, to the extent that it was compelled to announce its withdrawal from the League of Nations. At the time of deciding on this important event, His Majesty the Emperor issued an imperial rescript, clearly declaring the path that our country should take. The rescript stated:

"Japan, now that 'Manchukuo' is newly established, respects its independence and promotes its healthy development as the basis for removing the roots of disaster in East Asia and ensuring world peace. Furthermore, while I have always desired the establishment of international peace and have never ceased to do so, I will continue to cooperate with all countries in all peaceful endeavors. Although we are now separated from the League of Nations, in accordance with what the Empire believes, we are certainly not neglecting the friendship of friendly nations by focusing solely on East Asia. It is my constant concern, day and night, to have great faith in international affairs and to manifest great righteousness throughout the world."

The people of our country should henceforth work together in unity and strive to live up to the imperial will. Then, the Empire's bright and upright attitude will surely be thoroughly understood by the world, and the Empire's future will be full of brilliance. When I handle foreign relations, I will follow this imperial rescript and devote all my efforts to "thinking of world peace and implementing our country's policies through diplomatic means." Fortunately, the Empire's relations with friendly nations have become even closer and more amicable in terms of diplomacy and trade after our withdrawal from the League of Nations. I am extremely gratified.

Assisting Manchukuo's Independence

Since its founding, "Manchukuo," which has a close and special relationship with the Empire, has been steadily advancing its construction, thanks to the wise rule of Emperor Puyi and the unremitting efforts of the country's government, as well as the Empire's assistance based on the spirit of the Japan-Manchukuo Protocol. Various facilities are gradually being put in place, especially the maintenance of its public order, the development of industry and transportation, the establishment of its finances, and the progress of its education. Not only can it demonstrate remarkable achievements, but the issue of the imperial system, which the country's government and people have been looking forward to, is also about to be realized. The foundation of this newly independent country is becoming increasingly solid. This is not only something for "Manchukuo" to celebrate, but also for the peace of the Far East and the peace of the world. We must continue to follow the instructions of the imperial rescript, and the government and people must work together to provide vigorous assistance to the country's development.

Singing the Praises of Good Neighborliness with China

The Japanese government believes that it has a major responsibility to maintain peace in East Asia, and it has a firm and unwavering determination to do so. It believes that the stability of China itself is the most important situation for peace in East Asia. Therefore, it is the sincere hope of the Japanese government that China will quickly restore its public order and prosperity. It can be said to be the natural mission of China and Japan to maintain good-neighborly and mutual relations and to contribute to the peace and development of East Asia. However, when we look at the Chinese political situation, it is still far from the realization of such hopes, which is extremely regrettable. According to the information we have received, the Chinese government has only recently realized that the anti-Japanese policy it had adopted in the past was wrong and has decided to open up Sino-Japanese relations. However, as of today, we have not been able to find concrete facts to prove this information. If China understands Japan's true intentions and sincerely expresses its sincerity, then Japan has long been willing to fully accommodate China's goodwill and attitude. The fact that the area north of the Yellow River is maintaining a relatively peaceful state under the control of the Political Affairs Reorganization Committee is gratifying. In view of the contiguous relationship between "Manchukuo" and North China, and in order to maintain the armistice agreement in North China, the Japanese government is particularly concerned about the maintenance of its public order and hopes that no disturbances will occur. At the same time, the Japanese government is paying close attention to the activities of the Chinese Communist Party and the rampant activities of the Communist armies.

Adjusting Relations with Russia

Looking back at the diplomatic relations between Japan and the Soviet Union, since the establishment of the Basic Treaty of Beijing in 1925, the two countries have maintained normal contact. Even after the Manchurian Incident, they were able to understand each other's positions and did not encounter the occurrence of difficult problems. However, the Soviet Union's recent attitude towards our country has not only given us a sense of some changes, but the Soviet Union has also frequently released criticisms of our country to the inside and outside through news and communications, deliberately publicizing the deterioration of the situation and using it for its internal affairs and diplomatic work. This is something that Japan is deeply surprised and regrets. The Japanese government has always taken a fair attitude towards the Soviet Union, whether before or after the Manchurian Incident, and has always been consistent and unchanged. Although Japan and Russia have fundamental points of incompatibility in terms of national system and ideology, they always seek to continue good-neighborly relations and strive to resolve doubts by peaceful means. After the establishment of "Manchukuo," the adjustment of the diplomatic relations between Japan, "Manchukuo," and Russia, based on the directly contiguous border, is considered the most necessary belief for peace in East Asia, and we continue to work towards this. Although it has been publicized by the Soviet Union, the Japanese military has not built any new military installations on the Manchu-Russian border. In addition, the Japanese government has been mediating the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway for the past year since June, which is also in line with the implementation and purpose of this policy. The Japanese government is confident that the Soviet Union will soon understand our country's sincerity. Although the negotiations for the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway are currently suspended, we hope that the negotiations will resume soon.

Easing Feelings with the United States

Next, considering the relations between Japan and the United States, it can be said that there are no fundamental problems that are difficult to solve between Japan and the United States. Japan has always sincerely hoped to maintain good-neighborly relations with the United States and has no intention of deliberately creating incidents. At the same time, it is deeply believed that the United States will not hesitate to understand Japan's position in East Asia. However, since the Manchurian Incident, public opinion in the United States has tended to deteriorate, leading to a sense of emotional estrangement between the two peoples. However, because Japan has no other intention than to establish lasting peace in East Asia, if the United States can recognize the special circumstances of East Asia to some extent and understand the reason why our country is the power for peace and stability in East Asia, then the tension in the relations between Japan and the United States will naturally ease. This is undoubtedly the case. Therefore, Japan sincerely hopes that the two countries will understand each other deeply in view of the important relationship in trade and commerce, enhance the historical friendly relations, and create an atmosphere of peace and tranquility between the two great neighbors across the Pacific, which is both in name and in reality.

Expecting Friendly Relations with England

Although the traditional friendly relations between Japan and the British Empire have not been shaken today, the two empires are in similar geographical positions in the Eastern and Western oceans, and the two empires understand each other's positions in all aspects of the world and jointly contribute to world peace. In this sense, we adjust the interests in the issues of trade and commerce, and expect the increase of friendly relations between the two countries. The difficult trade issues that have arisen between Japan and India, an important member of the British Empire, have fortunately come to an end, which is something to be greatly celebrated by both sides in the overall situation.

Eliminating Trade Barriers

Looking at the recent world situation and international relations, it is easy to lose normalcy due to political unrest, economic turmoil, and ideological confusion. It is regrettable that the sense of mutual trust among the people of the world has also weakened as a result. If all countries are open and honest, and understand each other's positions, and promote the great spirit of cooperation among all nations, then the solution of any problem will not be too difficult. I believe that it is important for all countries to improve the habits of suspicion and exclusion, and to enhance the concept of mutual trust and cooperation. However, in terms of trade and commerce, there is no sign of any easing of trade barriers, but rather a worsening trend of increase. The World Economic Conference held in London previously also failed to achieve its expected goals and was disbanded. Recently, as a result of Japan's extremely developed industry, trade has greatly increased. However, many foreign countries have continued to restrict general trade and set up various obstacles to the overseas expansion of Japanese goods. The Japanese government is studying appropriate countermeasures to this. The government believes that mutual understanding of each other's unique cultures is an effective way to enhance understanding between countries. Therefore, in this area, we should respond appropriately to implement appropriate facilities.

Encouraging National Cooperation

As mentioned above, it is undeniable that Japan's foreign relations are full of challenges in the present and future. In general, when a country's strength is rising, it encounters many incidents. Therefore, our people should work together in unity and persevere. No matter what difficulties we encounter, we should have unwavering awareness and preparation. At the same time, we should implement just policies and take moderate actions with a calm and determined attitude. Then, not only will Japan have no need to feel uneasy in the future, but its future will be full of hope.

Relying on Military Force as a Backing

In short, we must never lose sight of the fact that Japan bears the full responsibility of being the sole cornerstone for maintaining peace in East Asia. Japan's diplomacy and national defense both arise from Japan's important position and responsibility. The very nature of Japan's national defense is both completely defensive and self-defensive. At the same time, Japanese diplomacy also seeks to consistently implement just and reasonable claims based on Japan's mission. I believe that Japan's natural and realistic position will be understood by all countries in the world as a matter of course. (23rd United Press Telegram)

Japan's Honeyed Words and Hidden Daggers: Britain and Italy Express Skepticism

Military Control of the Regime Exposes Aggressive Ambitions

(London) The Times of London stated in today's editorial that while the resignation of Japanese Army Minister Araki may herald a shift in Japan's foreign policy, there is currently no clear evidence of such a trend, but one cannot help but hope for it. The civilian politicians of Japan are indeed unable to avoid complaining about the enormous expenses required for maintaining security in Manchuria and preparing for war by the navy and army. However, they ultimately failed to reduce the second-largest budget in Japanese history. Foreign Minister Hirota's speech may somewhat alleviate the anxieties caused by this policy and Araki's remarks. For instance, if progress can be made in the negotiations between the Soviet Union and "Manchukuo" regarding the Chinese Eastern Railway, Hirota's statement that Japan has no hostile intentions towards Russia will be even more powerful. All Englishmen who read Hirota's speech cannot help but feel that his remarks were defensive in nature. Japan's aggressive actions in Shanghai, Manchuria, and elsewhere, even to its allies in Britain, are unsettling, and there is a longing for clear evidence that Japanese politicians are truly regaining control over their national affairs and the destiny of their country. The Daily Mail of London stated that Japan's ambitions for a great empire in East Asia have now become even more questionable. Hirota's speech directly reveals to the world Japan's intention to bring all of China under its control under the pretext of stability. Fortunately, Japan's imperialistic ambitions, even if not factual, may lead to its self-destruction in the course of implementing such grandiose plans. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

(London) The Manchester Guardian criticized the resignation of Japanese Army Minister Araki in today's editorial, stating that Araki's military prestige and insatiable rhetoric have placed him in a prominent position for the past two years, but his colleagues do not entirely obey him, as evidenced by Araki's proposal to convene an international conference on Far Eastern affairs. It also stated that Foreign Minister Hirota's remarks, at first glance, seem to indicate that the Japanese government is now eager to verbally appease the Soviet Union, but the value of these remarks can only be proven by actions. This is nothing more than a credible embellishment for Araki's resignation. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

Rome: The Italian people were pleased to hear Foreign Minister Hirota's statement in the Diet today that Japanese policy is peaceful and that there is no intention to prepare for war against Russia. Japan's activities in the Far East have long caused considerable anxiety in Italy. A new competition in naval armaments is about to begin, and a war between Japan and Russia with Vladivostok as its objective is highly probable. It is reported that when Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov passed through Italy on his way back to Russia from the United States, he had a detailed discussion on this matter with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. Although the Italian people are pleased to hear Hirota's remarks, they feel that concrete evidence is still needed if Russia is to be reassured and if the United States' naval armaments are not to increase further, as general opinion believes that Japan has already caused the United States to become alarmed about the security of its territories in the Pacific. Italian newspapers have recently repeatedly mentioned the dangers in the Far East, and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini himself has repeatedly called on Europe to deal with them. As far as Italy is concerned, the so-called dangers are mostly in the commercial field, as Japan has intense competition with Italian merchants in the market. Italians believe that the section of Hirota's speech today that referred to the disruption of the world market and commerce was largely caused by the Japanese themselves. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

Saito's Policy Speech

Supporting Puppets as the Central Policy

Advocating National Rejuvenation Through Hardship to Encourage the People

(Tokyo) The Japanese Diet reconvened this morning. The Upper House convened at 10:14 AM. Prime Minister Saito and Foreign Minister Hirota successively delivered speeches. The Prime Minister concluded by saying that Japan is currently experiencing internal and external difficulties, that is, a time of emergency. A time of national crisis is a time for national progress. The people must redouble their determination to overcome this period of trial. (China United Press dispatch, 23rd)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Saito delivered a speech on his policy direction in the Upper House this morning. The outline of his speech is as follows: The birth of a prince at the end of last year has further solidified the foundation of Japan, which is a great honor for the entire nation. Foreign policy will adhere to the principles of the edict issued at the time of withdrawing from the League of Nations on March 27 of last year, maintain friendly relations with all foreign countries, and assist the development of the new nation "Manchukuo" as Japan's most important mission. Supporting "Manchukuo" is based on Japan's fundamental national policy of maintaining peace in the Far East, and at the same time, it can maintain world peace. Japan's relations with all countries in the world remain unchanged. As for the budget for the ninth year of Showa (1934), a tight fiscal policy will be adopted. The total amount is 2,211,200,000 yen. Due to the economic recovery, natural tax revenue increases are expected. Increasing taxes is not yet the right time, so the shortfall will still be covered by issuing public bonds. However, the details will be explained by the Minister of Finance. During this period of global economic recession, since Japan lifted the ban on gold exports, the economic situation has been very good, and trade has been uniquely prosperous. However, the wounds of the rural areas have not yet recovered. Although efforts have been made to seek relief methods since last year, further efforts are still needed. National thought is becoming increasingly extreme, and the people must pay more attention to this matter. The government has taken measures to correct this since last year, making every effort to guide thought and study countermeasures. The Ministry of Education has also newly established an Education Research Department to intensify the study of policies. The government will continue to adopt the Rice Control Law as its principle and seek ways to raise rice prices. (China United Press dispatch, 23rd)

Takahashi's Speech on Finance

Huge Budget Deficit

Issuing Public Bonds to Make Up for the Shortfall

(Tokyo) The House of Representatives convened at 1:00 PM today. After the Prime Minister and Foreign Minister delivered their speeches, Finance Minister Takahashi took the stage to deliver a speech on financial policy. The content first explained the outline of the revenue and expenditure budget, and then stated that if ordinary revenue were used as revenue, there would be a huge shortfall. However, because the government considered the current economic situation, it did not reach the time to implement tax increases or establish other plans to increase revenue. In accordance with last year's method, public bond funds were used to offset the revenue shortfall. The Finance Minister then explained the public bond issue, stating that Japan's economic situation is gradually improving, and a large amount of natural revenue increase can be expected in Showa 9 (1934). From this evolution, it is expected to return to the revenue situation of Showa 3 and 4 (1928-1929) soon. However, Japan's finances not only have a large revenue shortfall, but also require very careful consideration of their future. Therefore, the number of public bonds issued must be drastically reduced. The necessary national defense expenses, which cannot be avoided in an emergency, are also calculated according to the principle of saving. As for other expenses, it is impossible to include them arbitrarily, which is truly unavoidable. The people must endure and strive for the future of our country, regardless of revenue or expenditure, and officials and the people must work together to overcome difficulties. The Finance Minister then spoke about the general economic situation in Japan, explaining the general rise in prices, the current situation of foreign trade, and the recovery of national purchasing power and savings. He stated that bank deposits increased by more than 710 million yen last year, and postal savings and trusts also increased by 100 million yen and 160 million yen respectively during the same period. He then stated the government's low-interest policy and talked about the current situation of foreign trade, saying that last year Japan's foreign trade exports were 1,920 million yen and imports were 2,014 million yen, totaling 3,940 million yen, and the trade deficit increased by more than 18 million yen compared to the previous year. However, from the perspective of overall trade, the amount and volume have increased significantly. Finally, the Finance Minister talked about the general trend of the world economy, saying that at present, there are very few countries that adhere to the principle of fair treatment in international commerce, and the world economic situation is still chaotic. Under these circumstances, it is fortunate that Japan's economy has signs of improvement in all aspects. However, the people still need to work hard to reach the stage of complete recovery. The people must forget their private interests and hope for Japan's eternal prosperity. (Japan United Press dispatch, 20th)

Massive Budget Proposed

(Tokyo) Finance Minister Takahashi submitted a budget proposal to the Diet today, stating that the expenditures for Manchuria, emergency relief, exchange losses, and the large increase in national defense expenses caused by the international situation have resulted in a huge shortfall in the budget proposal. The increased expenses cannot be offset by tax revenues. All tax revenues, except for capital taxes, have increased. The total increase last year was 131 million yen. Next year's expenditures for Manchuria will total 163 million yen. Other expenditures are as follows: Emergency relief 125 million yen, Army 110 million yen, Navy 190 million yen, Foreign exchange losses 80 million yen, totaling 2,112 million yen for national expenditures. Since Japan's current economic situation is not suitable for increasing taxes, it is proposed to issue bonds of 881 million yen, which is a decrease of 131 million yen compared to the public bonds raised last year. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

Diet Launches Questioning Offensive

Tokonami Takes the Lead in Scourging the Government

(Tokyo) At 2:33 PM today, as Finance Minister Takahashi finished his speech, Tokonami Takejiro of the Seiyukai immediately took the stage amidst applause, launching the first arrow of his questioning, intending to give the government a warning scourge. The gist of it is as follows: Since the current cabinet was formed, a year and a half has passed. Judging from its political achievements during this period, there is indeed room for various discussions, but in this autumn of national distress, it is necessary to acknowledge that it has passed through many difficulties. Secondly, a comprehensive review of the government's policies in diplomacy, finance, economy, industry, etc., especially in diplomatic relations, is intended to maintain Hirota's proposition and wish it success. Finally, he discussed parliamentary politics and opinions scourging the government as follows: If political parties can demonstrate their regeneration and improvement, the true face of parliamentary politics will surely be revealed. As for the current cabinet's policy direction, there is no established situation. Its enthusiasm and courage for the current situation are still lacking, and it has failed to exert its function as an organic entity. Many of us hold this feeling, which has become the main cause of political instability and public unrest. In this regard, I hope that the Prime Minister will pay special attention, exert his fearless spirit, implement his ambitions, and achieve decisive means. Since the Saito Cabinet was established based on this belief, it is necessary to explain the national policy to the people, which is what we believe is necessary. Please reply clearly as to what the government's will is on this matter.

Prime Minister's Reply Was Evading the Core (Tokyo) Prime Minister Saito rose to reply, saying, "Thank you very much for your attention. The policy direction stated by the government is the preparation for future implementation. I fully agree with what Mr. Tokonami said."

Tobu Questions Rural Problems Next, Mr. Tobu of the Seiyukai took the stage and questioned the rural problems, especially focusing on the Rice Control Law, asking, "Does the government have the courage to implement rice monopoly?" He also said, "It is a pity to neglect the rural problem for the sake of national defense."

Minister of Agriculture and Forestry Goto replied to Mr. Tobu's question, saying, "This year is expected to be a bumper harvest, so the implementation of the Rice Control Law still needs to be slightly considered, but there is no intention to revise it."

Minister of Colonial Affairs Nagai also replied. Mr. Tobu questioned again. The meeting adjourned at 5:24 PM.

New Army Minister Attends the Upper House Today, the new Army Minister Hayashi Senjuro attended both the Upper and Lower Houses, and made a simple reply in the House of Peers, which attracted much attention because it was his first speech. (Japan United Press dispatch, 23rd)

Keijo: According to the Korean military authorities, at 11:30 PM on the 22nd of this month, 300 members of the Liaodong Righteous Army crossed the Yalu River and invaded a certain location in Pyonganbuk-do, Korea, attacking the Japanese troops guarding the border. The Japanese troops were defeated. By the time reinforcements arrived, the Righteous Army had obtained ammunition and retreated to their original location. (China United Press dispatch, 23rd)

New Wine in Old Bottles: Hayashi Senjuro Assumes the Post of Army Minister

Reminding Saito Makoto to Pay Attention to Two Points: Resolving to Implement the Strong Hardline Policy

(Tokyo) Army General Hayashi Senjuro, Inspector General of Military Education, entered the Imperial Palace at 9:00 AM this morning. (China United Press dispatch, 23rd)

I hope you will pay more attention to this point. (Den Tsushin dispatch, 23rd)

Young Military Officers Unanimously Support

(Tokyo) The trend of the army after General Hayashi took office as the new Army Minister seems to be following the fundamental policies of former Army Minister Araki, that is, the army will not be re-selected, except for the regular changes in March to August. The new Army Minister Hayashi has the same honest, upright, fair, and selfless character as former Army Minister Araki, and also has the decisiveness that former Army Minister Araki lacked. Hayashi Senjuro, the New Japanese Army Minister

First New Move to Refresh the Military Department

Two Kinds of Observations Influencing the Political Situation

One Says That From Now On, the Country Will Be Able to Purify the Anxious Air

Another Says That the Crisis of Conflict Between the Government and the Military Will Increase

(Tokyo) Regarding the change of the Army Minister, combining the opinions of the political parties, the people, and the Upper House, it is said that the Diet has a considerable aversion to the words and actions of former Army Minister Araki. On the issues of military discipline and budget, they were prepared to pursue them deeply. This sudden change of Army Minister has the feeling of being unexpected, so the Diet can maintain calmness. Those who hold an optimistic view say that the faction represented by former Army Minister Araki has withdrawn from power, and the military's interference in politics is also not as good as before, so it can sweep away the atmosphere of political unrest. Those who hold a pessimistic view say that recently, the radical elements in the military department have gradually stopped supporting the Army Minister, and the demands within the department have gradually shifted to General Hayashi. Judging from this fact, in the future, the intentions of these radical elements can be expressed by Army Minister Hayashi. Erudite General Masaki Succeeds as Inspector General of Military Education

Araki is Reappointed as Military Councilor

(Tokyo) This morning, after the ceremony of appointing the new Army Minister Hayashi in the Phoenix Room of the Imperial Palace, the appointment ceremony of General Masaki as Inspector General of Military Education and General Araki as Military Councilor was held simultaneously. British Empire Naval Conference Discusses the Pacific Situation

Far East Fleet Generals Gather in Singapore to Prepare Defense of Territorial Security Plans

Singapore: The British Empire Naval Conference opened here today, with extreme secrecy. After Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota issued a declaration of self-defense, and the United States advocated building 120 new warships, the atmosphere is filled with uncertain signs. Representatives of the Navy, Army, and Air Force held an important preliminary meeting at the beginning of the month. This conference will have a far-reaching impact on British naval policy in the Far East. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

Singapore: The British Empire naval community is worried about the security of territories in the Far East. Generals of the Far East Fleet gathered in Singapore today to discuss the increasingly dangerous situation developing in the Pacific. Participants in the meeting included Vice Admiral Trelawny, Commander-in-Chief of the China Fleet, Vice Admiral Nasmith, Commander-in-Chief of the East Indies Fleet, Vice Admiral Hyde, Commander-in-Chief of the Australian Fleet, and Rear Admiral Waterhouse, Commander of the New Zealand Fleet. It is learned that the conference decisions will not be announced at all. Although military circles routinely deny that it has any significance, this is the first Imperial Conference in the Far East in five years, and it coincides with the new naval competition in the world. Since 1921, there has been no large-scale shipbuilding as much as today. According to statistics here, there are 30 powerful cruisers, 4 giant aircraft carriers, and several fleets of destroyers and submarines under construction. Japan and the United States are at the forefront of the competition. Britain has also been preparing its battleships and cruisers to the maximum extent in accordance with the tonnage stipulated in the Washington and London treaties.

According to British naval experts, recent developments in the Pacific are creating a situation similar to that of 1920 to 1921, when the Washington Treaty was signed to limit the accelerated naval competition between the United States and Japan. Since the two countries implemented the "Great Navy" plan, the British believe that the naval competition at that time has shown signs of re-emergence. Britain currently has two major problems, so it feels this development is particularly important. The first problem is the fierce commercial war between Britain and Japan, which has destroyed the spirit of the former Anglo-Japanese alliance. The second problem is the 1935 Naval Conference, where Japan has formally declared its intention to demand equality with Britain and the United States.

The recent situation in the Pacific has long caused concern in Australia. As early as October last year, Prime Minister Lyons and his predecessor Prime Minister Hughes repeatedly urged to re-examine the Imperial border defense plan. Hughes said, "Australia is the most vulnerable country in the world to the enemy, because it is separated from a certain country with an expanding population in Asia by a single voyage. Britain no longer holds maritime hegemony, and Japan is no longer our ally. Australia must prepare itself." (National News Agency dispatch, 22nd)

United States Navy Can Soon Dominate the World

Plan to Build 121 Warships

Modernizing the Entire Navy

(Washington) Today, the Naval Budget Review Committee approved the Navy Department's budget proposal of 293,833,040 yuan and submitted it to the House of Representatives. As a result, President Roosevelt's plan for the world's strongest navy can be realized. At the same time, the Senate is also discussing Congressman Vinson's proposal. According to Vinson's proposal, the US Navy should build as many warships as possible in accordance with the naval conference limits. The current Navy Department budget plans to spend 1.8 million yuan to build one 8-inch gun cruiser and three 6-inch gun cruisers. After these four ships are built in January next year, the United States Navy will appropriately achieve the 5:5:3 ratio signed at the Washington and London Naval Conferences. The budget plans to add 1,800 naval soldiers, bringing the total number of the US Navy to 81,500, and plans to add 63 officers and 16,000 Marines. The budget also plans to allocate funds to add 142 naval aircraft, most of which are seaplanes. As for the 100 fighter planes recently purchased by the US Army for 7.5 million yuan, they are entirely for the Army and cannot be included in the naval budget. This budget amount is 23,221,533 yuan less than the Navy Department's annual expenses, and 1,585,148 yuan less than the budget estimate. The number of new ships added and repaired in this budget is quite large. (National News Agency dispatch, 22nd)

(Washington) President Roosevelt told guests today that he strongly supports the Vinson Bill, which calls for the construction of 120 new warships at an estimated cost of 616.25 million yuan, saying that the United States can no longer be a model for disarmament elsewhere in the world. The White House's support for building warships in accordance with the treaty is based on the expectation that Japan will demand the same large navy as Britain and the United States when the current naval convention expires in 1936. Vinson is the chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee and has agreed to work to get the bill passed as soon as possible at the request of the Secretary of the Navy. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd)

(Washington) There is no doubt that the House of Representatives will pass the naval budget of 285 million yuan. The government plans to go a step further and approve the five-year naval construction plan proposed by the House Naval Affairs Committee, with an expenditure of 380 million yuan, distributed over five years at 75 million yuan per year. Vinson, chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee, is the drafter of this construction plan. He expects that Japan will demand that its navy be equal to that of Britain and the United States when the London Naval Treaty expires. (Havas dispatch, 22nd)

(Washington) Rear Admiral Standley, Commander of US Naval Tactics, today criticized the naval supply bill being reviewed by the House of Representatives and detailed the darkness of the US fleet, saying that while the latest US battleships should be modernized, the condition of other battleships is not satisfactory. As for the aircraft carriers Saratoga and Lexington, they have now degenerated materially. The situation of the destroyers is also very worrying. It is doubtful whether the destroyers can effectively perform their duties in wartime. The airship Los Angeles is no longer safe and may soon have to be dismantled. The naval supply bill requires 284,747,000 yuan, of which 33,619,000 yuan will be used to build new ships, including aircraft carriers and four cruisers. 18,880,000 yuan will be allocated to the naval air force, of which 6,131,000 yuan will be used to build new aircraft. As for the airship Akron, which crashed at sea last year, it is not planned to be rebuilt. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd)

Famous Generals of the European War Discuss British-Dutch Naval Alliance

Joint Defense of Far Eastern Territories; Japan's Issue a Great Worry for Britain

(London) The naval generals commanding the Australian Fleet, the New Zealand Fleet, and the British Empire's Far Eastern Fleet will begin a meeting today in Singapore Harbor to study appropriate methods for strengthening the British Empire's national defense. British General Allenby, a famous general of the European War, recently went to Java to consult with the Dutch authorities. In the event that British India, the Dutch East Indies, Australia, New Zealand, and other places are invaded, the British and Dutch navies will jointly resist. According to several newspapers, General Allenby will also participate in the Singapore meeting after returning from Java. It can be seen that the matters discussed at this meeting are particularly important. Furthermore, the opening of the Singapore Naval Conference coincides with the resignation of Japanese Army Minister Araki and the declaration by Foreign Minister Hirota. Therefore, the British newspapers are paying close attention to the issue of Japan's expansion of power. The Daily Herald, a Labor Party newspaper, stated that according to Foreign Minister Hirota's speech, there is no doubt that Japan wants to conquer and control the entire China. Placing the vast territory of China under the oligarchy of Japan, with its politics dominated and its economy exploited, would undoubtedly cause repercussions throughout the world. Fortunately, the desire for power alone is not enough to accomplish anything; it must be followed by practical efforts. However, if Japan still wants to strive to realize its grand plan of Japanese imperialism, its failure is highly probable. Nevertheless, for the present, we must immediately declare to Foreign Minister Hirota that while Hirota expresses a willingness to obtain our cooperation, Japan cannot expect our enthusiastic cooperation in this aggressive undertaking. The Times, a Conservative Party newspaper, takes a more reserved attitude, but the newspaper concludes that the issue of Japan, after a period of temporary silence, has now become a major hidden concern for Britain. Foreign Minister Hirota's speech provides further proof of this. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

League of Nations to Discuss Tense German-Austrian Relations

Austria Demands Germany Cease Disruptive Behavior

Fire on Parrot Island

Little Entente Conference

Unanimous Agreement on Recognizing Soviet Russia

Decision on Balkan Non-Aggression Pact

Bulgaria Notifies of Temporary Non-Accession

Zagreb, Yugoslavia The foreign ministers of the Little Entente countries held a meeting here and achieved very good results in just one day. According to a public statement, the foreign ministers' opinions were completely consistent. It was also stated that the foreign ministers have already adopted various decisions, but what exactly was decided was not clearly stated. This is because the evolution of the situation is extremely far-reaching, and the foreign ministers cannot help but speak cautiously in order to retain greater freedom of action. Czech Foreign Minister Beneš and Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu had consulted with Greek Foreign Minister Maximos in Geneva on the Balkan Non-Aggression Pact. According to reliable sources, Bulgaria has notified the Little Entente foreign ministers' meeting that it will not join the Balkan Non-Aggression Pact for the time being. Therefore, Greece, Romania, Yugoslavia, and Turkey will sign the agreement first. If Bulgaria wishes to join later, it will be allowed to do so. The public statement did not mention Russia at all because the three foreign ministers had already agreed on the recognition of Soviet Russia before the meeting, and only the procedural issues remained to be discussed. In addition, the Little Entente foreign ministers' meeting also decided to organize propaganda to resist the proposal to revise the peace treaty. Furthermore, the Little Entente Economic Conference held in Prague previously made various decisions regarding economic cooperation among the Little Entente countries. These decisions have now been approved by the foreign ministers' meeting, and the improvement of economic relations among the Little Entente countries has thus become a reality. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

Zagreb, Yugoslavia A fast train traveling between Berlin, Vienna, Zagreb, and the Yugoslav capital was near the Austrian city of Land when a bomb exploded in a first-class car. Five passengers were killed and one was seriously injured. Yesterday's telegram reported that Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu and Czech Foreign Minister Beneš were traveling on this train from Geneva, but the special car in which they were traveling had already passed Land long before the bomb exploded. It has now been determined that the bomb was placed in the car while the train was in Yugoslav territory. Whether the intention was to harm the foreign ministers of Romania and the Czech Republic, to show hostility towards the Little Entente countries, or to be a demonstration by a political exile is a question that everyone is asking. Last night, the foreign ministers of the three Little Entente countries already held talks on the train. This morning at 11:00, the first formal meeting was held at the local provincial governor's office. In the evening, there was another meeting. Afterwards, a public statement was issued stating that the foreign ministers of the three countries had discussed the issues of general disarmament, the Balkan Pact, and the relations between the Little Entente countries and their neighbors, especially with the Soviet Union. As a result, their opinions were completely consistent. The three countries believed that the movement to revise the peace treaty would cause ominous effects and decided to explain this to make people aware of it. (Havas dispatch, 22nd)

Zagreb, Yugoslavia The Little Entente Conference officially opened here at noon today, but the foreign ministers of the three related countries held a preliminary meeting last night, which did not end until 3:00 this morning. The Yugoslav ambassador to Austria also arrived here today. Although he claimed that he had no formal mission, it is generally believed that his trip was to report to the conference on the visit of Italian Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs Suvich to Vienna, as the Austrian issue is actually one of the most important aspects of this Little Entente Conference. It is also heard that it is feared that there will hardly be any concrete resolutions on any important issues at this conference, as the European situation has been changing a lot recently. Therefore, important matters can only be discussed and not dealt with for the time being. (National News Agency dispatch, 22nd)

Disarmament Talks at an Impasse; Germany Asks Britain to Mediate

To Propose a Compromise Solution Between France and Germany

British Government to Consider in Cabinet Meeting Today

(Paris) The German government has recently sent another official document to the British government, requesting the British government to put forward new suggestions in the hope of finding a compromise solution between the French memorandum and the Berlin reply. Britain originally decided to temporarily take a wait-and-see attitude towards the Franco-German negotiations before clarifying the German reply. Now that Germany has put forward this new official document, it has requested Britain to come forward to mediate before Britain has prepared any action. However, Germany's original views remain unchanged, and British political figures are not very satisfied with this. There have already been informal expressions of this. Therefore, Britain's assumption of mediation is not as easy as people generally imagine. While Germans in London have denied that their country has put forward a new official document, British public opinion is quite in favor of coming forward to mediate. Therefore, the Cabinet meeting on Wednesday will consider whether mediation can be realized. As for what the Observer reported yesterday, that the British government is preparing to put forward concrete suggestions on the number of land, sea, and air forces that each country can maintain, according to well-informed sources, this is completely inaccurate. (Havas dispatch, 22nd)

(Paris) This morning, the presidential palace held a State Council meeting. Because Germany's reply to the French memorandum relates to national defense, it was handed over to the three ministers of the army, navy, and air force for separate review. No further discussion was held. It is planned to make a calculation after each department has separately expressed its opinions on the technical aspects. Germany's reply continues to demand equal rights to armaments, regardless of the number of troops or military equipment, and that it must be implemented immediately. It also stated that Germany still believes that the French suggestion to reduce the French air force by 50% under certain conditions is not a sufficiently satisfactory concession, because Germany itself has no air force. It is generally believed here that although Germany's tough stance makes it impossible for countries to have any real hope of disarmament, it is also possible to establish a general convention stipulating that each country's armaments should be limited to the current number and that no further increase should be allowed. It is said that this idea was advocated by Czech Foreign Minister Beneš, the general rapporteur of the Disarmament Conference. In addition, the British Cabinet will hold a meeting on Wednesday to decide whether to put forward a compromise proposal again in accordance with Germany's request. At that time, the decision made by the British government may affect Germany's attitude. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

(Paris) The life of the French government is now in danger again, as a new case similar to the Bayonne affair has been discovered. The central figure in the new case is a bank founder and Prime Minister Alexandre, who is accused of defrauding no less than 2.5 million pounds. He was arrested today. The public's anger is unstoppable, because he has been the subject of much discussion for four years, and only today has he been arrested for questioning. It is feared in several quarters that the new case will seriously endanger the existence of the government. He was the subject of a report by the public prosecutor in 1930, and he should have been arrested at that time, but he relied on huge sums of money to influence police officers and was able to get away with it. Today, disturbances broke out again in front of the Chamber of Deputies, and the police stopped them with stern measures. Therefore, the public's resentment towards the police is even deeper. (National News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Paris) Since investigating the Bayonne public bond fraud case, Prime Minister Doumergue has taken prompt measures to rectify officialdom. A Glimpse of a Certain Foreigner's Drug Trafficking in Shandong Province

Selling Drugs Deep into the People

Worth More Than 200,000 Yuan in One Year

Jinan Dispatch: Heroin is ten times more potent than opium. In recent years, it has spread rampantly in various provinces of North China. Shandong, being a coastal province, has easy access to drug sources, making it particularly easy to penetrate the people. The provincial government has strictly ordered a crackdown and established addiction treatment centers. First-time offenders are forced to enter the center for addiction treatment. After being cured and released, their arms are tattooed to leave a permanent mark. Repeat offenders will be killed without pardon. In Jinan, the population is 400,000, but the residents live close together, with numerous police posts, making inspection easier. The atmosphere of drugs has not yet fully developed. However, the spread of drugs in the countryside is truly alarming. According to investigations, many foreign merchants along the Jiaoji Railway sell drugs wherever they go. All storefronts with the names "So-and-so Foreign Firm" or "So-and-so Pharmacy" are sources of drugs. East of Weixian, there is Huangqibao, a small place with only a few hundred households, which is extremely desolate. However, because it is close to the train station and is located at the intersection of Weixian, Changi, and Anqiu counties, transportation is still convenient. Several foreign merchants there sell drugs as an open secret, guaranteeing transportation and supplying the needs of nearby counties. In the past, people served tea to guests. Now, in addition to tea, they also offer drugs. This is necessary to show respect. They inhale wildly, feeling relaxed and happy. They even carry it with them while working in the fields, without any sense of shame. Even bandits demand drugs as ransom. The tragic situation is unbearable to witness. Rural areas are sparsely populated, making it difficult to conduct thorough inspections. Moreover, sellers and transporters are protected by foreigners. Although everyone knows, no one dares to do anything. Only Wang Honglie, the magistrate of Anqiu County, has enforced the crackdown more strictly. The drug situation in that county is lighter than elsewhere. It is reported that last year, villagers in Huangqibao held a theatrical performance to worship the gods for five days. Spectators from all directions gathered, and the sales of heroin surged. The daily transactions were constantly in the thousands of yuan. After the five days were over, the foreign merchants even funded the continuation of the performance for two more days in order to sell more drugs. It is estimated that from spring to winter last year, the money remitted by foreigners through post offices and other places, where the amounts were verifiable, reached more than 240,000 yuan. The amounts are unknown for larger stations and cities, which are hundreds or thousands of times more. They are all using drugs to harm our nation, while they reap huge profits from it.

The Course of the Guangdong-Guizhou Alliance

The Panjiang Conference First United the Internal Guizhou Army

The Nanzhai Conference Further Negotiated Between Guangxi and Guizhou

Scheduled Nanning Conference to Cope with the Situation

Guangzhou Dispatch: In recent times, the southwestern provinces have been paying close attention to contact with Guizhou Province in order to unite internally and seek development of mutual interests. Wang Jialie of Guizhou was originally a pro-southwestern element. However, Mao Guangxiang, Jiang Zaizhen, You Guocai, and others in Guizhou obstructed him, causing civil wars to break out in Guizhou. Wang Jialie was unable to attend to internal affairs, resulting in a failure to connect with Guangdong and Guangxi. Guangxi Province, being adjacent to Guizhou Province, was particularly concerned about Guizhou's internal affairs compared to other parties, and had jointly initiated a mediation of Guizhou's disputes with representatives from Yunnan Province, promoting Guizhou's unification, strengthening the southwestern unity, in order to cope with the situation. At the end of last month, Long Jiezhi, the representative of Guangxi, along with Fu Chuncao, the representative of Sichuan, Gan Jiayi, the representative of Guangdong, and Dan Maoxin, the representative of Yunnan, strongly mediated Wang Jialie and You Guocai, and both sides convened two peace conferences in Panjiang, Guizhou Province, setting the following conditions: (1) Wang Jialie would telegraph the central government, commissioning You Guocai as the Commander of Qingxiang in Guizhou Province, allocating eight districts of Panjiang as You's stationed territory. The taxes and levies in the area would be collected by You to cover military expenses. If it was still insufficient, Wang Jialie would provide appropriate subsidies. In the future, they would not fight each other with weapons. (2) Che Mingyi's department would be reorganized by Chen Yuwu, appointing Chen as a division commander. The departments of Lei Mingjiu and Yang Qichang would all be under Chen's control, designating Fenghuang and Tongren counties as their garrison area. (3) Jiang Zaizhen's department would be designated to be stationed in Zheng'an and Yanhe, under the control of Deputy Commander Hou Zhidan. In the future, Chen Yuwu and Che Mingyi of the Eastern Route, You Guocai of the Western Route, and Jiang Zaizhen of the Northern Route would all be under the command of Wang Jialie of the 25th Army. Wang Jialie would still be in charge of Guizhou's administration. It is heard that the above matters have been signed by all parties, and the representatives of the various provinces have also left Panjiang. The internal situation in Guizhou has temporarily become consistent. Wang Jialie, in order to further contact Guangxi Province to discuss various issues, had an appointment to meet Li Zongren in Nanzhai County, on the border of Guizhou and Guangxi. On the 10th of this month, Wang left Guiyang with eighty guards, driving directly to Nanzhai. Those travelling with him included Zheng Shao Cheng, the head of the Finance Department of Guizhou Province, Secretary General Li Wei Bai, and Xiong Guan Ying, the head of the Guizhou Highway Department. Li Zongren then went with Zhang Yun Liang, the representative of Guizhou and Chief of Staff of the Guangxi Army, as well as Shi Fang Bai and others. After Wang and Li met, they stayed at the Nanzhai County Government. It is reported that as a result of the consultation, there were concrete plans for the future transportation and economy of the two provinces of Guizhou and Guangxi, and the practical connection between Guizhou and Guangdong. On the 12th, Wang and Li bid farewell. Li Zongren took the road through Nandan, Hechi, Yishan, Binyang, and returned to Nanning. After Li returned to Nanning, he recently convened a formal meeting of several southwestern provinces in Nanning to seek the great unity of the southwest, to discuss consistent strategies to cope with the situation, and to jointly issue consistent proposals. A telegram has been sent to Wang Jialie, Mao Guangxiang, Jiang Zaizhen, You Guocai, and Che Mingyi of Guizhou Province, as well as representatives from Yunnan and Sichuan, inviting them to participate. The Husha Steamer Had an Accident

The Husha steamer, which operates between Shanghai and Taicang, is dedicated to transporting goods for various merchants in our county. At around 3:00 AM the day before yesterday, the steamer was towing five cargo ships from Shanghai back to Taicang. Due to a moment of carelessness, the first and second cargo ships struck a large anchor and sank immediately, causing a loss of more than 10,000 yuan. The goods mainly came from Shaxi and Huangjing. Wuxi

Cold Weather and Frozen Ice Disrupt Traffic

The weather has been severely cold in recent days. The indoor temperature has dropped to around 30 degrees. Water drips turn into ice. The day before yesterday, coupled with the howling north wind, the rivers in the city and countryside were completely frozen. Steamboats under the Gongyun Bridge, such as the Tongfeng of the Yangxian Company, the Yixing steamer, and the Huaxin and Yufeng steamers of the Yonggu Company, which travel to Yili, all sailed to Shuanghejian and then returned due to the ice. The other steamers operating routes to Fangqiao, Zhou Tieqiao, and Gushan also returned halfway. Only the steamers operating routes to Suzhou and Changshu were able to pass by breaking the ice, as the ice was slightly thinner along the way. The smaller steamers in the countryside were mostly suspended. Luggage piled up like mountains at the steamboat wharves, making it difficult for passengers to move forward or backward. However, passengers traveling from the city to Luoshe and Shitangwan all changed to trains. The various merchants in the city have also been greatly affected by the suspension of shipping.

Kidnapped Hostage from Suzhou Rescued in Changzhou

The home of Shen Chunjiang, a villager near Xiaoxi Town outside the Loumen Gate of Suzhou, was recently robbed. Shen's son, Gengsheng, was also kidnapped. The hostage was then hidden on a small boat, which sailed to Guanghua Bridge outside the Xiaonanmen Gate of Changzhou. On the morning of the 22nd, a river patrol noticed that the situation was suspicious and reported it to the Nanyunzhen Patrol Team and the Second Police Station of the Public Security Bureau. It was later discovered that a coal ship was also involved in the case. Police were dispatched to search and capture Wang Ayun, Wang Yunlin, Li Zhiyou, and Xu Xiande, among others, who were taken to the station and detained. Li Haokang, a patrol officer at the Second Police Station, also learned that the bandits had been negotiating a ransom in Shanghai. Gu Binchun was sent to Suzhou to notify the family to come to Changzhou to retrieve the hostage.

Robbery and Murder Case in Wangdian

The home of Dong Maosheng in Hewawan, about three miles from Wangdian Township in Jiaxing, was suddenly attacked by seven or eight bandits late the day before yesterday. They carried two muzzle-loading guns, while the rest carried ironware, wooden sticks, etc.

They broke into the inner room and searched at will. Then they went to the room of Dong Yongxiang, Maosheng's nephew, to search and rob. Although Dong was over sixty years old, he was still strong and powerful. He resisted the bandits. One hired worker and one neighbor were also seriously injured as a result of fighting the bandits. The bandits

then went southwest, with a total loss of several hundred gold pieces.

Young women Cheng Lanying and Wei Haihua, dressed in fashionable coats and leather shoes, accompanied by a man named Zhong Shunchun and others, were smuggling a large quantity of red pills, twenty-three bags weighing ten jin and seven liang, and two small packets of opium, weighing two liang. They were traveling from Hangzhou to Yuhang by a small bus of the Daya Company. They were discovered by the inspectors and police when they passed through Liuxia. Since the case involved opium prohibition, they were sent to the Hangzhou District Court for interrogation. After the interrogation, an order was issued to send them to prison for strict handling.

He was arrested by the police and sent to the court for questioning. He was prosecuted for theft in violation of Article 337 of the Criminal Law. Zhou Xingfa was found guilty of burglary and sentenced to six months of imprisonment.

Young Traveler Commits Suicide by Taking Poison

A young traveler suddenly arrived at the Xintai Hotel in the Xinshi Market of Hangzhou yesterday (the 22nd) at 2:00 PM and booked Room 89. He claimed to be from Ningbo, named Bao Yuqiao, 22 years old, and a merchant. After dinner, he went to bed. He had not gotten up by 11:00 AM this morning. The waiter knocked on the door but received no response. He suspected something was wrong and broke into the room. He saw that the young man's face had turned pale. Next to him was an empty bottle of sleeping pills. Knowing that he had taken poison, he immediately sent him to the Municipal Hospital for treatment.
