The Trend of Rent Increase in Shoupin Lane on Huade Road Is About to Expand

Since receiving letters from the Gao Yi Public House rental office requesting rent increases, the tenants of Shoupin Lane on Huade Road have unanimously decided that in this time of economic depression and social and economic decline, the original rent is already a burden. Now, the rental office, disregarding public opinion, wants to increase the rent by as much as 150%. They commissioned lawyer Yuan Yang'an to reply on their behalf, requesting that the rent increase proposal be withdrawn. Recently, tenants in the lane have reported that the Gao Yi rental office is first threatening to stop paying for the supply of tap water and other expenses, and now is threatening to demolish the houses. Yesterday, the head of the construction team who previously built the houses in the lane came to inspect, and stated that as soon as the notification is received, he will start building bamboo fences, etc. The tenants were shocked upon hearing this. After discussion, they still commissioned lawyer Yuan to represent them and sent letters to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association and the Municipal Council, asking for help and relief, and publishing the facts of the case in newspapers and soliciting assistance from all walks of life.

Development of Home Electrification

Everyone marvels at the wide use and great effectiveness of electricity in factories, transportation, and traffic. However, with the advancement of modern science, the use of electricity began with electric lights and gradually increased, leading to the realization of home electrification. Electrification means that everything, big or small, uses electricity to replace the labor of the past. The convenience of electric lights is known to all, and for daily sweeping, there are vacuum cleaners to serve people, which are both clean and hygienic, and convenient and labor-saving. All household necessities, such as irons, floor scrubbers, water boilers, and bread toasters, can use electricity to save laborious work. Electric heating has even greater uses, such as electric stoves in winter, which have no ash and no smoke. Electric stoves in the kitchen make cooking convenient and unparalleled. Electric refrigerators protect food and are unsurpassed. Furthermore, electric water heaters provide a constant supply of hot water all day long. All kinds of electric heating can save the trouble of cleaning up ash and dirt, and have the convenience of obtaining heat in an instant. Therefore, an electrified home can obtain all kinds of advantages such as comfort, hygiene, convenience, and labor-saving. Today, there are no less than tens of millions of families building this kind of home, and it is certain that in the future, it will increase to hundreds of millions.

The Reaction to the Rent Increase in Penglai Market

The shops in Penglai Market on Penglai Road in this city were notified by the landlord Kuang Zhongmou that starting from January of the 23rd year [of the Republic], the rent for each room would be increased by five yuan (the rent for the 22nd year was twenty yuan), making each room twenty-five yuan. The tenants strongly opposed this, saying that they could not afford it in this time of economic depression. They elected representatives to negotiate with Kuang to avoid the increase, but to no avail. They had no choice but to hold a meeting to discuss countermeasures, but there was no result. Yesterday afternoon, the tenants held another meeting at the Yingbin Restaurant teahouse in the market, and elected the female owner of Wuzhou Pharmacy, Shu Peizhen, as chairwoman, and Zhou Jianzhai as secretary. They stated that the rent for the 19th year was ten yuan, for the 20th year it was fifteen yuan, for the 21st year it was not increased due to the war, and for the 22nd year it was increased to twenty yuan. This year, they asked the landlord to postpone the increase but were not granted permission. The whole body decided to join the Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee and await a public decision. As for the rent for January, it will all be deposited in a bank for safekeeping, and the landlord will only receive the rent after the matter is resolved.

The Second Zhenru Qingzhen Villa Was Completed Yesterday

There is an increasing number of Shanghai Muslims traveling to and residing in Shanghai. The Rizhui Port Cemetery in Hebei has already been filled. Although there is vacant land in Henan, it suffers from being low-lying and surrounded by factories, which is gradually becoming unsuitable. In recent years, the religion has purchased a lot of land north of Gujiazhai in the Zhenru area, some for public cemeteries, some for charitable cemeteries, and some for private property. However, the biggest regret is that there is only a cemetery and no mausoleum. When the coffin is brought to the cemetery, there is no place to rest. If it rains or snows, even the mourners have no place to stand. The directors of the Shanghai Qingzhen Board of Directors, Ha Shaofu, Jin Xusheng, Su Zixiang, and Wang Hairu, in view of this, initiated the construction of the Second Qingzhen Villa, continuing and expanding the name of the Rizhui Port Villa. After years of preparation and months of construction, it has now been completed. Yesterday, a completion ceremony was held. Many cars departed from the Fuyou Road Mosque, and about a thousand people attended. Various Muslim organizations sent representatives to participate. The meeting opened at 10:00 AM. First, Imam Ha Desheng was invited to recite the first chapter of the Quran to show the intention of prayer. Next, Imam Da Pusheng gave a lecture on religious doctrine, which was extremely profound. Next, Director Su Zixiang reported on the construction situation and the accounts in great detail, and commemorated the contributions of Jin Xusheng's maternal uncle, Ma Yitang, to the Second Villa, which moved the listeners. Afterwards, guests spoke one after another. After the meeting, refreshments were served, and everyone dispersed happily. On the day, the traffic on the road was heavy, and it was quite a grand occasion for a time.

Clock Shop on Xinzha Road Robbed

Time: Yesterday at 5:50 PM

Loot: 100 Watches Worth 1300 Yuan

Yesterday at 5:50 PM, two robbers suddenly arrived at a clock shop at No. 595 Xinzha Road. One robber was unarmed, and the other was armed with a gun. The armed robber entered the shop and shouted at the staff and apprentices in the shop, forbidding them from making any noise, and drove them into a corner to keep them under control. The unarmed robber opened the counter, and all the cash and foreign currency stored inside, totaling 1,300 yuan, were robbed. The robbers were still not satisfied, and opened the clock cabinet, and also robbed 100 valuable wristwatches and pocket watches. They went out and fled. When the staff came out, the robbers had already fled far away. They immediately ran to the Xinzha Police Station to report the incident. The police station sent detectives to investigate the scene and ordered detectives to search and arrest the robbers.

The weather in this city has been severe for the past week. The temperature on the Fahrenheit thermometer has dropped to around 20 degrees. The tap water on the roads and alleys in various places is frozen. Although the sun was seen yesterday morning, the afternoon was suddenly cloudy and densely covered. For a time, snowflakes flew, sometimes sparse and sometimes dense. According to general expectations, it will snow heavily.

Hu Biao Yong An Tang Establishes a Lending Center for Unemployed Compatriots

Mr. Hu Wenhu, the owner of Hu Biao Yong An Tang, invented four kinds of effective medicines, including Tiger Balm, to benefit the world. Based on the charitable spirit of helping the distressed and relieving disasters, he has provided a great deal of assistance to charitable causes abroad. Recently, the national situation has deteriorated, and there are many unemployed people. The owner is deeply saddened by this. Mr. Hu Guiyu, the manager of the Shanghai branch of the hall, is also kind-hearted and willing to help. Seeing that various parties have jointly organized relief efforts for the unemployed, he has undertaken the grand purpose of the hall's owner and independently established a lending center for unemployed compatriots to make a living. Each person only borrows five or ten yuan, which is simple and easy to implement, and provides a lot of assistance. It can be called a savior for the unemployed. The declaration and the simple regulations are recorded below:

Declaration The Shanghai Branch of Hu Biao Yong An Tang Announces the Establishment of a Lending Center for Unemployed Compatriots to Make a Living, stating that in today's world, when economic depression is rampant, the unemployment wave has swept to our country. Not only are the farmers in the countryside economically exhausted, but also the unemployed workers in the cities are numerous. If relief is not sought quickly, people will be trapped by their livelihoods, take risks, and disrupt society, which can shake the foundation of the country. Although the way to relieve the situation depends on the fundamental plans of the government and cooperation, we cannot turn a blind eye. In view of this, this hall has taken the liberty of establishing a lending center for unemployed compatriots to make a living, with the general office located at the Shanghai branch of this hall, and branch offices located at the general agency offices and special management offices in various foreign ports. Several provisional borrowing regulations have been drawn up and published below, so that the unemployed can borrow this to earn a little for clothing and food, and avoid the urgency of hunger and cold. It is clear that a drop in the bucket is of no avail, but if society has one less unemployed person, then the country will have one more law-abiding person. We dare not talk about the fundamental way to solve the problem, but the superficial plan will definitely have a slight effect. At the beginning of the establishment, there are many imperfections, and we hope that experts will not hesitate to give guidance.

Simple Regulations Simple Regulations of the Lending Center for Unemployed Compatriots to Make a Living Attached to the Shanghai Branch of Hu Biao Yong An Tang. 1. The name of this office is the Lending Center for Unemployed Compatriots to Make a Living Attached to the Shanghai Branch of Hu Biao Yong An Tang. 2. The purpose of this office is to relieve unemployed compatriots and help them open up a way to make a living. 3. The general office is located at the Shanghai branch of Hu Biao Yong An Tang, and the branch offices are located at the general agency offices and special management offices of this hall in various places. 4. Any citizen of the Republic of China who is over 18 years old and under 50 years old, physically fit and hardworking, has no bad habits, and is truly capable of making a living but has lost the opportunity to make a living, regardless of gender, can borrow a livelihood fund of 5 to 10 yuan from this office. However, this borrowing can only be used to sell Tiger Balm products and cannot be used for other purposes. 5. When borrowing money, in addition to the borrower filling out a voluntary application, a reliable shop must be found as a guarantor. 6. The borrowing limit is temporarily set at 300 people in this city and 50 people in each foreign port. If necessary, the situation may be considered and the amount may be increased. 7. The loan is to be repaid interest-free within six months. If it cannot be repaid by the due date, the guarantor will be pursued. 8. If the first loan is repaid, and you want to borrow again, you should submit another guarantee. 9. The borrower must report the sales situation to this office every day and add new goods with the money earned. If the performance is excellent, a bonus will be awarded after six months to encourage them. 10. If the borrower stops selling Tiger Balm products midway due to an event, they must report to this office and return the borrowed money. If the products have not been sold out, the products can be converted into cash. 11. If the borrower uses the name to deceive or cause trouble outside, once verified, the borrowed money will be recovered from the guarantor. If the circumstances are serious, legal sanctions will be taken. 12. If these simple regulations are found to be imperfect, they may be modified by this office and notified.

Note Tiger Balm products are effective in treating diseases and have been widely praised as essential items for home and travel. Therefore, they are easy to sell and do not require a large amount of capital. For example, borrowing six yuan from this office can purchase one dozen each of iron box Tiger Balm, Bagua Dan, and Headache Powder. Using one day's time, you can sell them in the alleys, residential areas, wharves, stations, or teahouses, restaurants, bathhouses, and theaters. At a minimum, you can sell the above goods, earning two yuan for each yuan of profit, which is an income of one yuan and two jiao. And if an unemployed person sells medicines, they will surely be deeply sympathetic to the buyers, giving great convenience to the sales. Those who have tasted the bitterness of unemployment may wish to try it.

Another report states that Tiger Balm is effective in treating frostbite, according to those who have used it, so the sales of this oil have recently increased sharply. The hall has telegraphed the Shantou factory to send a large batch, which is expected to arrive in this city soon.

The China National Cotton Cloth Market is the textile and cloth barrier that followed the iron and steel barrier, with the purpose of relieving hand-made cotton cloth workers and resisting Japanese yarn and cloth. The National Traditional Medicine Industry's Petition Representatives Return to Shanghai Satisfactorily

The national traditional medicine industry believes that in recent years, foreign forces have invaded, greatly affecting the traditional medicine industry, and there is a lack of people to promote it and no help for improvement. It specially sent representatives Chen Xunqi, Ding Haoying, Cai Tonghao, Fang Ningjian, and others, totaling more than 50 people, and the entire medical and pharmaceutical community in the capital, to the Central Party Headquarters to petition, requesting a clear order for equal treatment between traditional Chinese and Western medicine, etc., and there was even a threat to collectively strike if the goal was not achieved. A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency went to inquire yesterday about the leaders of the traditional medicine industry in this city, and their remarks are as follows:

Seeking Improvement Through Equal Treatment

According to the talk, a certain member of the Central Committee once proposed abolishing traditional Chinese medicine, which would not only be an insult to national essence, but also affect the welfare of the people. Traditional Chinese medicine practitioners are determined to ask the central government to maintain it and present various points in detail to seek promotion from a high position, issue a clear order for equal treatment with Western medicine, and benefit the development of the national medicine industry. The representatives are determined that if they cannot get what they want, they will only resort to the final strike to fight for the way out for traditional Chinese medicine.

Petition Representatives Return Satisfactorily

The traditional medicine industry in this city sent representatives Cai Tonghao, Cen Zhiliang, and Fei Yongzu to Beijing to participate in the petition. The matter has now been completed and they have returned to Shanghai. The results of the petition are generally satisfactory. The Secretariat of the Congress expressed its acceptance of all points of the request and agreed to submit them to the Fourth Plenary Session for discussion and decision.

The Southwest Responds with Perseverance and Striving for Survival

The Executive Committee of the Southwest also telegraphed the Fourth Plenary Session in Beijing, proposing to stipulate equal treatment between Chinese and Western medicine, and other places have continued to express their support for the petition. However, traditional Chinese medicine does have some shortcomings, and practitioners are now determined to find ways to improve, persevere, and strive for survival.

The Directorate General of Posts Announces Continued Acceptance of Ordinary Mail to Xinjiang

However, Air Mail is Temporarily Suspended

Surface Mail to Blocked Areas Will Be Forwarded

The Directorate General of Posts of the Ministry of Communications announced that because the turmoil in Xinjiang has not yet ended, the postal routes have been cut off, and mail cannot be delivered. All air mail via the Eurasian Aviation Company's Northwest Line had been previously announced to be temporarily suspended. However, because the remaining ordinary mail can still be sent, and as for the blocked locations, the bureau specifically issued a notice stating, "It has been found that the postal routes in Xinjiang are completely blocked, and mail communication has been suspended. All kinds of mail to Xinjiang received by the post office before are now temporarily滞留en route and cannot be delivered. Except for airmail that needs to be delivered via the航綫 west of Gaolan, which should be temporarily suspended, the post office can still accept ordinary mail to Xinjiang that is not airmail, and transport it to the blocked locations first. As soon as the postal routes are restored, it will be forwarded immediately. This is announced to the public." Postmaster Zha Peilin.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends a Letter to the Railway Bureau to Open the Iron Gate in Front of Kenghai Road on the Railway

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Two Railways Administration yesterday, stating, "Respectfully, on the 21st of this month, we received a letter from the Changzhou Shanghai Fellow Association stating that according to reports from a large number of factory worker members, there was a convenient gate on the opposite side of the iron gate on the boundary road of the North Railway Station near Kenghai Road. Recently, for some unknown reason, the railway police used wire to block the gate. Although there is a main entrance, it is dozens of steps away. The [convenient gate] will only be opened when the train is about to depart. Therefore, it is inconvenient. Shanghai is a major port for Chinese and foreign communication. Except for times when the situation is unstable and martial law is ordered, such a phenomenon may occur. Now that the situation is peaceful, why is there such a situation suddenly? Please kindly ask the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to request the Municipal Government and the Railway Administration to quickly open [the gate] to facilitate transportation, etc." According to this, the Standing Committee of the association decided to submit a letter to the Railway Bureau, requesting that the matter be investigated and that the Municipal Government and the Railway Administration be allowed to open [the gate], which would be a great service. We have found that there was an open gate on the boundary road of the North Railway Station near Kenghai Road, which was convenient for pedestrians. Once closed, not only is transportation hindered, but also passengers taking the train are inconvenienced. Is it possible to open it as usual to facilitate transportation? According to the foregoing situation, we hereby send a letter to your bureau for investigation and reply.

The Dredging Bureau Sends Personnel to Germany to Supervise the Construction of a Dredger

The Dredging Bureau needs a large drawer or automatic dredging wheel to open up the灘 outside the Wusong Estuary. Because there is no such large shipyard in our country, it has ordered one from a certain steel factory in Germany, with a construction cost of about 4.8 million yuan and a one-year term. If the performance is excellent, a second one will be ordered. A Gas Pipe Explodes, Three Workers Poisoned and Injured

A few days ago, the Shanghai Gas Company's main factory suddenly exploded while testing a new gas pipe, injuring and knocking down several workers on the spot, as reported in this newspaper. Unexpectedly, at about 8:00 AM yesterday morning, a gas pipe suddenly exploded at No. 2524 Yangshupu Road Lan Road, inside the factory's new plant, while the workers were working. Three workers next to the pipe, Gao Yousheng, Wu Qifa, and Wang A'er, were hit first and fainted from the gas. The engineers of the factory, upon hearing the news, quickly closed the gas valve and notified the police, who rushed to send a fire brigade ambulance to take the three poisoned workers to the Sacred Heart Hospital for emergency treatment. However, because the injuries were very serious, their lives were in danger.

Fire on Da Xi Road

Around 9:20 p.m. the night before last, a fire broke out at the home of Shen Qu, a native of Dongtai, next to the Jianchang Construction Factory in Wangjia Lane, Da Xi Road, in western Shanghai. The fire was caused by a child playing with a candle, which ignited and quickly spread to the roof. In a short time, the fire spread to the flat rooms occupied by the material watchmen next to the factory. Neighbors made every effort to put out the fire, which was eventually extinguished. A total of two flat rooms were destroyed. Officers from the Sixth District Patrol Station went to the scene to investigate and detained Shen Qu for questioning in the Sixth District.

Huilo Company's Winter Sale: Since the start of the winter sale at Huilo Company, located at the corner of Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road, customers have been very crowded. The company is limited to selling all its inventory as much as possible within this month, and prices for all items have been greatly reduced, from 20% to 90% off. The company does not consider profits and only seeks to clear out its stock. With the deadline approaching, any remaining unsold inventory will be further reduced from the already discounted prices. Items such as women's gloves, scarves, cashmere socks, and the famous Battersby brand felt hats are now selling for only ten and a half yuan each. Fountain pens are being sold at half price according to the original price code. All items are exceptionally cheap.

All of its Black Cat brand products, such as ties, bow ties, shirts, and all Western-style clothing items, have been sold in society for a long time and enjoy a great reputation. Because its products are excellent and its prices are low, everyone who wears Western-style clothing likes to use them. Peide Company has now received letters from all walks of life requesting a winter discount sale. This is a rare opportunity for those who want to buy high-quality and inexpensive Western-style clothing items.

Various famous books are being sold at discounts ranging from 50% to 75%, and gift certificates with actual value are being given away to facilitate the study of social sciences.

Publishing World

Letter

To the Editor: Recently, your esteemed newspaper published an article about the Taikoo Shanghai-Hankou-Wusong steamer company's expulsion of middle-class workers last year. The article stated that the Seamen's Union had scheduled a general meeting of representatives of various ships at the Middle-Class Public Office on February 1 to discuss the entire plan. This is inconsistent with the facts. The Seamen's Union had already established appropriate measures for the Wusong steamer case, but Taikoo refused to accept them, so it has been delayed until now. We are currently actively negotiating. As for the representatives' meeting on February 1, it was initiated and convened by our office to rectify all internal affairs of our department and has nothing to do with the Wusong steamer case. I hope you will check and correct this. Sincerely, Zhou Xiaoting, Wei Xie Sheng, and Wang Ou Min, Standing Committee Members of the Jianghai Steamer Middle-Class Public Office, January 22.

Reading Q&A

How to Train Our Brains (1)

Reading Guidance:

After reading the articles in your column on the 13th and 14th, I was awakened, because I am someone who is "lost in the sea of learning, not knowing what to choose" and "wants to study Einstein's theory of relativity without even understanding elementary algebra." Therefore, when I accidentally want to learn a certain subject, the result is always that I retreat because the "subject is too specialized." I have bought many natural science books, but because I don't have the corresponding basic knowledge, I end up wasting money. Now I am raising a reading question, and I ask you to reply to me with a letter.

Now, I will first describe my personality, environment, etc., so that you can understand me.

(1) Personality: I am a person with low intelligence, fond of low-level interests, often having pointless fantasies and delusions, and also careless, cowardly, and slow. When I was in school, my math grades were often failing, but I did very well in memorizing and writing Chinese and English. I am not interested in sports.

(2) Level: I dropped out of the old system of middle school in the second grade to go into business. While in school, I did not understand math at all. After leaving school, because of self-motivation, I actually completed an arithmetic textbook on my own (half of the credit goes to the detailed answer explanations). I wanted to pursue algebra, but it was too difficult, so I stopped halfway. Then I started to study English on my own and it was very effective. Because I finished Li Taen's English reader on the Three People's Principles, I already had some ability to read English newspapers. Therefore, I continued to work hard. Now, for the Miller's Review and ordinary English literature books, I can read them as long as I have a dictionary in hand. For things that are easy to understand, I often like to translate them into Chinese. I am very interested in Nash's Grammar Fourth Book. Because I am often with English books, I have a habitual fondness for English.

Environment: I work as an accountant in a shop in a rural town, earning a few dozen yuan a month. English is of no use here, but my personality is the opposite.

Hope: Because I am good at low-level interests, after repeated efforts to reform, reading famous Western literary works and biographies of historical figures, etc., I have gradually changed my inferior thoughts. But I hope to cultivate a brain that is organized, rigorous, sensitive, and sound. I dare not have any ambitions, I only hope to be qualified to be someone who understands the times, a healthy citizen, and a people with a scientific mind.

What I am asking for guidance here is: (1) What subject will make my brain rigorous and sound, sensitive, and eliminate pointless reverie and delusions?

(2) Logic can organize our thoughts, but can someone who has not learned algebra and geometry understand it on their own?

(3) Is it better to learn formal logic or dialectical logic?

(4) Should I give up English and pursue other urgently needed subjects because I am afraid that "in the end, I will not be proficient in foreign languages, and I will not gain anything from the subjects I want to read"? (Letter from Xu Lezhen)

Mail forwarding: 1. Yao Tianyou, Shi Renjun: Please indicate a communication address so that we can reply by letter.

Essays

On Success and Failure

— Ban Shun

Whether I can accomplish an ideal event depends on whether I have a strong will and ability. Of course, this seems to be a "cliché," so why should I dwell on it? However, if we observe from a philosophical perspective, there is still room for discussion.

The ancients said it well: "Where there's a will, there's a way." Then, this is what is called "success." At the same time, there is a saying: "Pride comes before a fall." This is what is called "failure!" Let us look at the former's so-called spirit, which is a kind of "cultivation" of a certain event. Using this kind of cultivation to concentrate and work, there is no doubt that nothing cannot be accomplished. However, if there is no cultivation under this statement, and one cannot be as calm as an old monk in meditation, then even if his spirit is concentrated, it will inevitably overflow. Without cultivation, one's energy will inevitably overflow. It is true that it is like a young monk who is difficult to attain enlightenment, and it is not easy to succeed in a great undertaking, which is a pity. At the same time, the word "overflow" also means "to show it to the outside." To show it to the outside is pride. Pride is the overflow of energy. As the Shanghainese say, "not up to par," then failure is inevitable.

Therefore, the success or failure of a career depends entirely on whether people have a unified spirit. No matter what they do, as long as they are "enthusiastic," it is not difficult to judge their success or failure. The so-called "enthusiasm" here, in popular terms, is "dedication," which is also the meaning of "unified spirit." The unification of spirit lies in the result of "deliberate attention." This deliberate attention is essential for us and is a kind of perseverance. Only with perseverance can there be a manifestation of genius. If one is self-proclaimed a genius but lacks the will of perseverance, it is also in vain. Especially young people with vigorous blood, many lack the concentration of attention; otherwise, with the self-mastery of not moving or being confused, the attention of not yielding or being intimidated, and the absence of fear of difficulty or complacency, hum! hum! I guarantee you will succeed immediately.

Therefore, in discussing the "success or failure" of a career, the arrival and unification of the spirit is a necessary process for a great undertaking; otherwise, it is difficult to succeed. Therefore, I have written this essay on success and failure to appeal to those who sympathize.

Laziness

— Li Min

We Chinese people used to be in the limelight and contributed to culture. Each era has its own spirit, so we boasted of being the "Celestial Kingdom," the king of the world, and the rest were barbarians and insignificant countries. But now, we are looked down upon by foreigners. What is the reason?

Originally, our people suffer from a disease, which is "laziness!"

Our people do not like to interfere in other people's affairs. Everyone is afraid of trouble. The bad ideas of "one thing less is better than one thing more" and "sweep the snow in front of your own door and don't care about the frost on other people's roof" are deeply imprinted in their minds. This bad psychology of "too lazy to care about other people's affairs" allows traitors, warlords, corrupt officials, local tyrants, and evil gentry to act illegally and do all kinds of evil. China is suffering from an incurable internal disease.

Our people are too lazy to interact with others, so there is no unity. It's like a pile of loose sand. Someone said, "Accumulate sand into a tower," but sand has no "stickiness" and cannot be a tower. It's like people lacking emotion cannot accomplish anything. Our people lack this emotion - the spirit of cooperation - so there is no great undertaking, let alone development.

Our people get by as best they can, and one day is counted as two and a half days. This lazy mentality leads to a lack of creativity. When they see that other people's things are selling well, they make counterfeit brands. Even if you get away with it, how is our own thing compared to others? Our people know how to enjoy themselves, but they cannot endure hardship. They are too lazy to do anything. They cannot build airplanes, they cannot build trains, they cannot build guns and cannons... They buy what other people have discarded. How can they compete with others? How can they fight with others? How can China become rich and strong?

One national humiliation after another is coming. Our generous people, who can support a boat in their stomachs, are too lazy to argue with others. But, compatriots! Do we have to wait until the fire is burning our eyebrows, or when we have to shit, we cannot but shit to realize that we cannot do this?

The Leisure Class

— Yan Chonglou

People who are unwilling to work and do not have to work are called the "leisure class." Originally, people all hated work and loved leisure, but because of the pressure of hunger and cold, people have to rack their brains and shed blood and sweat to maintain their lives.

The "leisure class" outside the labor circle will not experience the panic of hunger and cold. They have money to solve all problems. Their lives are too idle! So they have to come up with all kinds of entertainment methods to dissipate this excess time.

"Those who sit idly by cannot eat." Although the book clearly tells us this, some people witness that the "leisure class" can not only sit idly by and eat, but also sit idly by and enjoy all the pleasures (?). Then the psychology of "getting something for nothing" arises! All kinds of evils in society also arise!

The laboring people are too laborious, and the leisurely people are too leisurely. This forms an inverse proportion, which is the struggle of classes. It would be best if people could all become the "leisure class." Then it would be comfortable, but all production would be cut off. What kind of world would this be!

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 23: The Pain is Unbearable, Concentrating on Listening to the Music; The Joy is Not Satisfied, Hastening Farewell with Flying Talismans.

This day at noon, several wooden pillars were erected on their roof, and people were setting up a shed there. According to Beijing custom, when people have weddings, funerals, or birthday celebrations, they must erect and set up a shed in the yard, so that they can use it as a temporary auditorium under the shed, which is commonly called "handling affairs." The family across the street had no one celebrating a birthday, no one giving birth to a child, and no one dying. This must be a wedding. If there was to be a wedding, then naturally, Zhao Ziqiang had returned home, and Guizhi was getting married. With such an omen, the number of times he went out for a walk each day increased. The next morning, after washing, he seemed to be urged by someone, and immediately ran outside the gate, looking at the passers-by. But he didn't need to think too much. On the gate of the Zhao family, there was a piece of bright red and dazzling material with words written on it, namely "Auspicious Match, Marital Harmony." Above the door frame, there was also a red paper horizontal plaque, namely "The Star of Happiness Shines High." When Ji Zhi saw it, he couldn't help but sneer. The meaning was, what is an auspicious match, does anyone in the Zhao family still have Gan Zhi in their heart? As for marital harmony, hum! I don't think there will be such a day. As long as Zhao Ziqiang doesn't drop his gun, he can't live the life of a couple at home. He criticized the festive couplet in secret, but he refused to leave and stood in the doorway of his own gate to watch the excitement of other people's families. At this time, a person who specializes in handling tea and water for people's affairs set up a tea stove as big as a vat at the entrance of the Zhao family, and five red lacquer carved tea tables were placed on one side. Above it was a glass frame, and below it was a printed tablecloth. Hundreds of teapots and teacups were placed on the table. This is also a peculiar custom of the old capital. When people have happy events, they specially find this kind of person to manage the tea and water. Ordinary people put this kind of arrangement outside the gate. Although this is said to avoid taking up space in the yard, it is actually a kind of show-off, so that people know there are many guests. (298)

Vendor of Wonton Soup

— Yang

Hearing the distant clacking sound of the wonton vendor's bamboo instrument... my stomach felt a pang of hunger, and I hurriedly opened the door to await his arrival.

It was indeed early winter: at night, before ten o'clock, the streets already appeared strangely desolate and lonely. Only the late-night congee shops, due to their business needs, were still standing alone in this cold wind. All other shops were quietly closed. Looking from one side of the street to the other, one could hardly spot a soul. Occasionally, someone would pass by, their head and neck shrunk in, their face sallow—obviously just out of their warm home. The northwest wind came in gusts, now tight, now slack, terribly cold, and blowing on me, I couldn't help but shiver!

Under the dim, yellowish street lamp, I saw him carrying his heavy-looking shoulder pole, walking step by step!

After a round of calls, he set down his pole. A smile spread across his weathered face as he asked, "Sir, how many would you like?" His accent was not like the locals, even though he was trying, it sounded strangely grating. "Thirty will do!" I said, handing him the bowl.

So, he began his work. Seizing the opportunity during this idle time, driven by curiosity, I casually asked, "You've been doing this business for many years!"

"Almost four years now," he replied, as he placed the wontons into the pot.

"Your accent doesn't sound like a local; where did you move from?"

This was an unintentional question, but it touched a sore spot for this middle-aged man. He sighed, "Ah, sir, you don't know! My hometown was originally in Jiangxi, but the Communists destroyed it all! My wife and children are scattered, and I'm all alone, drifting to this place. This business, from dusk till late at night, is not fit for a human! The more he spoke, the more agitated he became, almost shedding tears.

After hearing his words, what way could I find to comfort him?

When he had cooked the wontons and handed them to me, he picked up his pole and left! I stood there blankly, watching the silhouette of this wanderer gradually disappear under the lamplight. A feeling of immense melancholy arose in my heart. May God forever bless this lonely soul!

Global Oddities

— Chen Donglin

The Funeral of a Foot

In Budapest, the capital of Hungary, a man named Marius Tiamon recently held a bizarre funeral for his foot. His right foot had contracted a stroke, so he followed the doctor's advice and had it amputated. However, according to Jewish religious customs, "Any part of the body that dies accidentally should be buried." Therefore, he followed this rule and placed the foot in a coffin, held a grand funeral, and buried it in the earth amidst the pastor's sorrowful prayers. It is said that this man cried loudly for a while during the burial. This can be said to be the world's most peculiar funeral.

Maintaining the Original Price of Virginity

Recently, a great commotion has arisen in the Sden region of Africa over marriage based on purchase. According to local customs, buying a bride requires fifteen head of cattle, but due to the recent poor climate, ordinary people of the non-propertied class cannot afford fifteen head of cattle. In light of this, the Sden government, in order to make marriage "popular," implemented a "social policy" of reducing the price of brides. As a result, the women of Sden were furious, posting slogans everywhere such as, "Maintain the original price of virginity," "Absolutely oppose price reductions," "The government should resign," and so on, and held large-scale demonstrations. They even planned to hold a national convention of virgins, making a great commotion. On the other hand, the proletarian youths launched a fierce opposition movement, leading to bloody clashes with the women. It is said that the government is currently still considering the matter.

God's Address

Seven years ago, a curious person in Leipzig, Germany, mailed a letter, with "God" written on the envelope. The local post office forwarded the letter to various places such as Rome, Greece, and Palestine, but the letter was recently returned to the sender's location. A slip of paper was attached to the letter, reading, "Addressee unknown"! Atheists were overjoyed to hear about this. And the letter with the attached note was bought by a wealthy man for five hundred marks.

A Century-Long Plan

The government of Angola recently resolved that officials who marry women from other countries will be dismissed, but the article of the decree notes: "If the woman from the other country is wealthy, then it can be tacitly approved." This can be said to be the humor of the Angolan government.

Island Without Germs

According to a recent conversation with Dr. Spinton, who returned to London after exploring Tristan da Cunha Island in the Arctic Ocean, although the island only has 150 residents, there has never been a patient on the island, so there is not even a doctor.

Doctor of Sound Effects

Recently, a very rare scholar appeared in the United States, named C. S. E. E. After investigation, it was found that this is an abbreviation for Doctor of Sound Effect Engineering. It means a Doctor of Sound Effects Engineering. His skill is to use musical instruments or other objects in front of the broadcasting station to produce sounds such as trains, footsteps, waterfalls, rain, waves, and the cries of animals and ghosts. It is said that this Doctor of Sound Effects is the first degree of its kind in the world.

Strange Commemorative Statue

Recently, a very peculiar commemorative statue was erected in a certain large park in Moscow. From the front it looks like Marx, from the right side it looks like Stalin, and from the left side it looks like Lenin! The intention is simply to mechanically place the three great founders of the Soviet Union together, so as to combine them into one!

Ministry of Education Orders Rectification of Gansu College

(Nanjing, 23rd) The Ministry of Education replied to the Gansu Provincial Government, ordering Gansu College to earnestly improve all matters concerning the improvement of Gansu College. The college should, together with the Gansu Provincial Department of Education, in accordance with the points raised in the consultation, consider local needs, manpower, and financial resources to quickly formulate a practical plan, and separately draft an organizational outline, and then report to the Ministry for review and decision. Before it has been approved, it must not continue to recruit new students by following the old organization. (Nanjing, 23rd) On the 23rd, the Ministry of Education replied to the Gansu Provincial Government, ordering Gansu College to earnestly rectify and abolish the affiliated middle school and primary school, eliminate political and art subjects, end the law department, and enroll students every other year, merge the literature department, and change the education department to the literature and history department, and the agricultural department should first establish a vocational department.

The Current Situation of Education in Anhui Province (3)

| Inspection Report by the Special Commissioner of the Ministry of Education, Li Ximou |

According to a recent survey, there are 131 public schools in various counties in Anhui Province. The Provincial Department of Education is actively urging its subordinate educational institutions at all levels to establish public schools as much as possible to promote public education. (The "Overview of the Promotion of Public Education in Anhui Province" compiled by the Anhui Provincial Department of Education is omitted here). The Anhui Provincial Department of Education has the following opinions on promoting public education: (1) The Provincial Department has achieved remarkable results in sorting out local education funds in previous years. According to the Provincial Department, local education funds in various counties should be thoroughly investigated and sorted out, and all the increased income should be used to expand the first phase of compulsory education and short-term compulsory education. (2) Compulsory education funds in the province have always been special funds, but in many counties, they have been used for other purposes. In the future, strict rectification and restrictions should be imposed so that all compulsory education special funds are used for compulsory education. (3) In various counties and villages in the province, it is rare to find thirty or forty households concentrated in one place. Therefore, village private schools can better adapt to environmental requirements and are more developed than primary schools. In the future, the promotion of compulsory education in rural areas should mainly focus on improving private schools. (4) According to the Provincial Department of Education, those who run education in various counties in the province usually only deal with official documents and respond to higher-level agencies. In the future, the implementation of compulsory education should strictly implement the assessment regulations for county magistrates and education directors. When provincial supervisors inspect various districts, they should also conduct practical assessments, and give awards and punishments to those responsible for education.

(7) The current situation of female secondary education. Judging from the number of existing schools, female secondary education does not seem to be very developed, but the demand for female secondary education is very urgent. For example, the Hefei No. 6 Girls' Middle School has been established for only a few years, and the increase in students every year has already shown one aspect of it. In terms of vocational subjects, there are subjects such as dyeing and weaving, sericulture, and embroidery, but household subjects such as sewing and cooking are not valued. There are currently six girls' middle schools in Anhui, each with three classes in senior high school and normal school. There are only two female secondary vocational schools, one in Anqing and one in Shouxian. The No. 4 Girls' Middle School has three vocational classes. According to the current economic situation of the province, the expansion of female secondary education is quite difficult. However, the Provincial Department of Education plans to establish a girls' middle school in Huailian, northern Anhui, in the 24th year. The current plan to change the setup of the girls' middle school is listed below: "First District" Anqing Girls' Middle School (newly reorganized) (central Anhui), Anqing Girls' Normal School (newly reorganized) Anqing Girls' Vocational School Embroidery Department will be closed and set up a sericulture and dyeing and weaving department, Anqing Girls' Midwifery School (planned to be established), "Second District" Huizhou Normal School (newly established), Huizhou Girls' Junior Middle School (gradually stopping enrollment of the normal school department of the Fourth Middle School), "Third District" Yingzhou Normal School (reorganized from the new Fifth Girls' Middle School and the senior high school department of the Third Middle School) Yingzhou Girls' Junior Middle School (reorganized from the Fifth Middle School), "Fourth District" Xuancheng Normal School (reorganized from the senior high school department of the Fourth Middle School, gradually stopping enrollment of the general department) (southern Anhui), Wuhu Girls' Middle School (reorganized from the Second Girls' Middle School, gradually stopping enrollment of the normal school department), Wuhu Private Vocational School (sewing and sock knitting are very suitable for social needs), "Fifth District" Fengyang Vocational School (reorganized from the Fifth Middle School) (central northern Anhui), the junior middle school department affiliated with Fengyang Normal School Huaiyuan Girls' Middle School (planned to be established in the 26th year, after its establishment, Fengyang Girls' Junior Middle School will be closed immediately), "Sixth District" Luzhou Girls' Junior Middle School (reestablished from the Sixth Girls' Middle School)

Luzhou Normal School (reorganized from the Sixth Girls' Middle School) Shouzhou Girls' Junior Vocational School of Engineering (the sewing department is changed to the home industry department).

(8) Implementation status of laws and regulations for primary and secondary schools (A) "Matters concerning secondary schools", (1) The political changes in the names of secondary schools: The names of middle schools, normal schools, and vocational schools in Anhui Province have not yet been fully corrected in accordance with laws and regulations, and are now gradually being carried out. (2) Reporting forms for secondary schools: The matters that each school should report and the reporting deadline have also been specified in detail by the Provincial Department of Education, and the forms and instructions have been printed and issued to each school to fill in and report on time, and the Department will verify and transfer them. (3) The distribution of recurring expenses of secondary schools: The budget for the 22nd year of the provincial secondary schools in the province has been compiled and submitted to the provincial government for approval and implementation. The distribution of recurring expenses of county-run private secondary schools has also been corrected in accordance with the regulations. (4) The appointment of principals and faculty members of secondary schools: Regarding the appointment of principals of secondary schools, since the first semester of this year, the province has separately followed the laws and regulations of secondary schools. Regarding the appointment of faculty members, the Provincial Department of Education has issued a form for faculty members to the provincial secondary schools, ordering each school to open a detailed resume of qualified personnel and submit it for verification. Faculty members who have not been approved by the Provincial Department of Education may not issue a formal employment contract. If the hired faculty members have unqualified qualifications, the Provincial Department of Education may order a re-appointment. As for the county private middle schools, the Provincial Department of Education has also strictly reviewed them to comply with the regulations. (5) The number of faculty members in secondary schools: The number of staff stipulated in the budget for this year in secondary schools in Anhui Province has

Compared with the 7th year, the number of staff has been reduced. As for the staff of county-run private secondary schools, the Provincial Department of Education also strictly reviews them when each school submits an outline budget and a list of faculty members. (6) The establishment of single-line laws and regulations and methods for secondary schools: The Education Department has now drafted methods for reviewing the income and expenditure of secondary school funds, methods for managing and awarding and punishing discipline, methods for calculating academic performance, the amount of student fees to be collected, scholarship methods, methods for faculty training, faculty salary scales, methods for increasing annual merit pay, and standards for subsidizing county private secondary schools, and submitted them to the Legal Committee of the Department for review. (B) "Matters concerning general middle schools", (1) The setting of vocational subjects in middle schools: The equipment in middle schools in the province is mostly simple, and vocational subjects have not yet been set up. It is now planned to actively increase the equipment in each school from this year so that it can be added as appropriate. (2) Middle schools also run spring semester classes. Very few primary schools and junior middle schools in the province run spring semester classes. The budget for this year has been approved. It may be impossible for middle schools in the province to add spring semester classes in the next semester. It is now planned to make a decision when compiling the outline budget for the 23rd year. (C) "Matters concerning normal schools", (1) The independent establishment of normal schools and the correction of names are in progress. The new establishment and names of normal schools in the province are listed below: "First District" Chizhou Normal School (reorganized from the first rural normal school, gradually increasing the enrollment of senior high school normal departments), Anqing Girls' Normal School (newly reorganized), "Second District" Huizhou Normal School (newly established), "Third District" Yingzhou Normal School (reorganized from the Fifth Girls' Middle School and the senior high school department of the Third Middle School), "Fourth District" Xuancheng Normal School (reorganized from the senior high school department of the Fourth Middle School), "Fifth District" Fengyang Normal School (reorganized from the Fifth Middle School), Bengbu Simple Rural Normal School (correct name from the Second Rural Normal School), "Sixth District" Luzhou Normal School (reorganized from the Sixth Girls' Middle School), Huanglu Simple Rural Normal School (newly reorganized), (2) There is no establishment of private normal schools in the province. (D) "Matters concerning vocational schools", (1) The separate establishment of vocational schools: Except for the provincial No. 4 Girls' Middle School, which has three classes in the junior vocational department, the provincial and county private secondary vocational schools in Anhui Province are all separately established. (2) Matters concerning the establishment of departments in vocational schools: The province plans to set up a farm in Sixian from the 23rd year to recruit training classes. The expenses will be subsidized by the province by half, and the rest will be raised by the commissioner. A forestry training class is also planned to be attached to the East Flow Education Public Forest Farm. From the 23rd year, Taihu and Fuyang counties will be assisted by the province by half to set up farms and training classes. The county private secondary vocational schools in the province, such as Hefei, Woyang, and Fuyang, are all single-department schools, but the Wuhu Private Anhui Vocational School has both mechanical and dyeing and weaving departments. (3) Matters concerning urging counties to set up junior vocational schools and encouraging private individuals to set up vocational schools: The province has stipulated methods for rewarding county-run vocational schools when formulating standards for subsidizing county private secondary schools. As for the existing county private middle schools, the province has strictly urged them to change to vocational schools in accordance with the order. (4) Matters concerning vocational school internship training, employment guidance, and years of study: The province has also ordered all schools to follow the regulations regarding the allocation of vocational school curriculum time, the expansion of internship sites, and internship methods, works, training methods, and employment guidance. (E) "Matters concerning primary schools" (1) Senior primary schools shall not be established separately. Very few primary schools in the province are established separately. It has been ordered that each county add junior primary schools in accordance with the primary school regulations, or merge with other local junior primary schools. In addition, the province paid special attention to this point when reviewing the outline budget of local education funds in each county this year, and issued separate instructions to correct it. (2) Unifying the names of primary schools: The provincial primary schools in the province are now named after place names. Private schools always use proper names. The experimental primary schools of the provincial middle schools and normal schools have also been renamed as affiliated primary schools of certain middle schools. As for the primary schools in each county, the province has ordered to unify the names, and there are fourteen counties, including Lai'an, that have reported in accordance with the order. (3) Unifying the jurisdiction of primary schools: No agency other than the educational administrative agencies in the province has been found to establish any primary schools. (4) Matters concerning the establishment of experimental primary schools: The experimental primary schools of the provincial middle schools and normal schools, and the experimental primary schools of each county have all been ordered to change their names. In the future, there will be only three experimental primary schools in the provincial capital. (5) Matters concerning the formulation of single-line methods for primary schools: Regarding this, the province has drafted methods for calculating the performance of primary school children in each subject, methods for examining conduct and physical education, and methods for promotion and demotion. The original primary school funds, auditing methods, and the minimum standards for the establishment of primary schools in each county have also been amended separately. (6) Matters concerning the collection of tuition fees by primary schools: The province has ordered each county and each primary school under its jurisdiction to follow the regulations, and pay close attention to it when reviewing the budget of each county and the establishment of each private primary school. (7) Matters concerning the organization of primary school education research associations: The province has drafted the regulations for the organization of research associations.

Local

Regarding the Resolution of the Current Student Unrest at Kwang Hua University

Ministry of Education Dispatches Zheng Hongnian to Nanyang to Inspect Education

Principal's Position Temporarily Held by Shen Pengfei

Stern Punishment Determined for Students Who Initiated the Unrest

Further Disturbances Will Be Reported to the Government for Severe Action

Mr. Shen Will Arrive in Shanghai Soon to Rectify School Affairs

(Nanjing, 23rd) Sun Ke, Executive Director of the Kwang Hua University Board of Trustees, wrote to the Ministry of Education, stating that the Board of Trustees held a meeting on the 19th to discuss and resolve the current student unrest. It was decided to send Principal Zheng to Nanyang to inspect overseas Chinese education and raise funds for Kwang Hua University. During his absence, the Ministry of Education is requested to send personnel to maintain school affairs and investigate and severely punish the students who initiated the unrest. The matter is duly recorded and submitted to the authorities for review and action.

Shen Pengfei Appointed as Acting Principal: Ministry of Education Announces on the 23rd

A Ministry order to Kwang Hua University states, in brief, that Principal Zheng Hongnian is being dispatched by the Ministry to Nanyang to inspect education and raise funds. All duties of the principal will be temporarily held by Shen Pengfei. At the same time, the Kwang Hua University Board of Trustees is requested to promptly designate representatives to join Ministry-appointed personnel to investigate and severely punish the students who initiated the unrest. On the 23rd, the Ministry of Education ordered Director-General of General Affairs Lei Zhen and President of Tongji University Weng Zhilong that the student unrest at Kwang Hua University has been ongoing for nearly two months, and the actions of some students have greatly exceeded the norm, causing deep distress. Without strict punishment, academic integrity cannot be restored. The Director-General and the President are hereby dispatched to join representatives of the school's Board of Trustees and the Dean of Academic Affairs to conduct a thorough investigation and report to the Ministry for review and action. The new Principal of Kwang Hua University, Shen Pengfei, stated that he would comply with the Ministry's order to go to Shanghai soon and expects to arrive at the school within a month to take office. The situation at Kwang Hua University is complex, and how to reorganize it will depend on the actual situation after arriving at the school, and then deliberate. It is heard that the position of Director of Higher Education at the Ministry of Education is vacant and will be temporarily filled by a Councilor. However, the candidate has not yet been determined.

Minister Wang Speaks: Minister of Education Wang Shijie stated that the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission have each sent personnel to investigate the current student unrest at Kwang Hua University. When reporters visited Minister Wang yesterday to inquire about the Ministry of Education's handling of the situation at Kwang Hua University, he said that the actions of some students during this unrest have greatly exceeded the norm. In recent years, the government has been striving to improve funding, facilities, and curriculum for various schools. Most schools have shown significant improvement in discipline compared to the past. However, Kwang Hua University has still experienced such a severe unrest, which is deeply regrettable. The existence of Kwang Hua University is of great importance. On the one hand, it provides a more convenient opportunity for overseas Chinese to study. On the other hand, it can maintain and foster the overseas Chinese's love for their motherland and their enthusiasm for the government. Only as a last resort would the Ministry be willing to see the school become unmanageable or be dissolved due to this student unrest. The school's Board of Trustees has also been very cautious in handling this matter. The Ministry has now decided to handle it according to the Board of Trustees' resolution. The students of the school should immediately realize this and restore the school to normal as soon as possible. If there are still disturbances, the Ministry, in order to establish a good academic atmosphere throughout the country, will not hesitate to request the government to take the most severe measures.

Results of This Year's Citywide Middle School Joint Entrance Examination Announced

Graduation Approved for 44 Senior High Students and 42 Junior High Students

Required to Repeat Grade: 32 Senior High Students and 23 Junior High Students

Statistics Show Natural Sciences as the Weakest Subject

Education Bureau to Award Scholarships to Top Three Students in the Joint Entrance Examination

This year's citywide joint entrance examination for middle school graduates was completed in early January. All test papers have been graded by the subject committee, and the Joint Entrance Examination Committee Office has organized and calculated the results, which were recently completed. The results have been announced by the City Education Bureau and published in a special issue to be distributed with today's Morning Post. The main points are summarized below.

Number of Examinees: A total of 4,441 students from 43 middle schools participated in this year's joint entrance examination for senior and junior high graduates. Among them, 1,221 students from 14 schools participated in the senior high graduation examination; 79 students from 21 schools participated in the senior high makeup examination; 992 students from 18 schools participated in the junior high graduation examination; and 149 students from 31 schools participated in the junior high makeup examination.

Examination Results: A total of 44 senior high students were approved for graduation, 45 were required to take supplementary courses, and 32 were required to repeat the grade. Among those who took the senior high makeup examination, 56 were approved for graduation, and 23 were required to take supplementary courses or retake supplementary courses. A total of 42 junior high students were approved for graduation, 27 were required to take supplementary courses, and 23 were required to repeat the grade. Among those who took the junior high makeup examination, 120 were approved for graduation, and 29 were required to retake supplementary courses.

Reward Measures: The Joint Entrance Examination Committee held a meeting yesterday and approved reward measures for schools and students with the best results. Students with a graduation score of Grade A (80 points or above) will be given a certificate of commendation. The first-place student in senior high will receive a scholarship of 50 yuan, the second-place 40 yuan, and the third-place 30 yuan. The first-place student in junior high will receive a scholarship of 30 yuan, the second-place 20 yuan, and the third-place 10 yuan. Schools must have all three grade levels at Grade B or above to be given a certificate of commendation to show encouragement. (The list of schools and students to be rewarded, as well as the list of students who passed or failed, can be found in today's special issue of the Morning Post.)

Overview of Performance: Statistics on the results of this year's joint entrance examination for each subject reveal some alarming trends. In the senior high examination, which covers nine subjects, physics ranked eighth and chemistry ranked ninth. In the junior high examination, which covers seven subjects, physics and chemistry ranked sixth and mathematics ranked seventh. This clearly shows that the performance of natural sciences in various middle schools is the worst. It is hoped that all schools will pay sufficient attention to this in the future. It is heard that the Education Bureau will select such subjects in the future and conduct random tests at various schools at any time.

Special Price Reduction for Transportation of Educational Supplies on State-Owned Railways

The Ministry of Railways Issues a Circular to All Railway Bureaus Announcing the Special Price Reduction Regulations for the Transportation of Educational Supplies on State-Owned Railways: Article 1: In order to support education and enlighten the public, the Ministry will charge a special reduced rate of 1.7 cents per 100 kilograms per kilometer for the transportation of textbooks, instruments, books, and printed materials used by schools, provided that they are specifically for educational purposes and are published or manufactured in China, regardless of the distance. If the weight is less than 100 kilograms, it will be calculated as 100 kilograms. Other educational supplies used by schools that are specifically for educational purposes and are deemed necessary to promote education may also be handled in accordance with these regulations, but must first be submitted to the Ministry for approval. Article 2: If there are textbooks, instruments, books, and printed materials used by schools that cannot be replaced by domestic products and must use imported products, the Ministry of Education or other highest local educational administrative agencies shall consult the Ministry for approval. Article 3: If the consignor wishes to pay fees in accordance with these regulations, they must submit the store's shipping invoice and tax payment receipt to the stationmaster for inspection when reporting the shipment. Article 4: If textbooks, books, or other goods not used by schools are mixed in the shipment in an attempt to save costs, once discovered, in addition to collecting the freight according to regulations, a penalty of ten times the first-class freight rate of the respective railway shall be imposed. Article 5: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (Note: These regulations were promulgated on the 20th of this month.)

Results of the Shanghai Municipal Council Scholarship Examination Announced

The Shanghai Municipal Council offers ten scholarships each year within its Chinese schools, determined by examination. The scholarship is equal to half of the annual tuition fee. Among the ten scholarships, four are awarded to male students from Council-run primary schools, two are awarded to female students from Council-run primary schools, and the remaining four are open to male students from all primary schools. This year's examination was taken by a total of 43 male students (34 from Council-run primary schools and 9 from non-Council-run primary schools) and 5 female students. All Primary Schools Should End Evening Gatherings Earlier

City Education Bureau Issues Order to All Primary Schools to Comply

No Later Than 9:00 PM

The Shanghai City Education Bureau yesterday issued an order to all municipal and registered primary schools in the city, stating that primary schools often hold gatherings of students and their families near the end of the semester or on commemorative dates to promote cooperation between schools and families. In order to take into account school courses, student academics, and family convenience, some gatherings are held after school or in the evening, often lasting until late at night, causing inconvenience. Moreover, most primary school students are young children, and it is especially inappropriate for them to be out too late. Therefore, if schools hold evening gatherings in the future, they must end them earlier, no later than 9:00 PM. All schools are hereby ordered to comply with this order.

Sports

Western Qing Basketball Finals

McLarens Still Submits to Pirates, Pirates Win Fifth Consecutive Championship

25｜35 Pirates' Defense is Like an Impregnable Fortress

Smith and Carlson Give Unique Performances

New Yang Defeats Mingqiang in First B-League Final

The Pirates continue to hold their fifth consecutive Western Qing basketball championship. McLaren's final efforts last night still ended in failure. The result of the game was 36 to 25, a difference of eleven points. The referee was Hall, and the inspector was Jessup.

Chinese basketball in the Western Qing League has been declining, unable to compete, and as a result, there are few patrons, even to the point of being deserted. Last night's final between the Pirates and McLarens attracted many Chinese ladies to watch, scrambling to get in. Of course, there were also many Western spectators. The Western Qing basketball hall was packed, the first grand occasion since the Western Qing basketball game between Lianghua and the Pirates. The game cannot be called exceptionally good, nor can it be called bad. The Pirates' victory was the inevitable result, as they were superior to McLarens in every way. Their tight defense was like an impregnable fortress, with no gaps to be entered. The victory also lies here, and McLarens must also sigh at their accurate long shots. McLarens are ultimately not as experienced. In the B-League final, New Yang defeated Mingqiang 56 to 27.

The Shanghai Basketball Association A-League is scheduled to begin on the 27th. In the future, the two teams will meet again twice, and we will see who is better. It is hoped that a strong and outstanding Chinese team will rise up and defeat them to regain face.

Reasons for McLaren's Failure

Before the game, it was said that McLaren could defeat the Pirates this year and win the championship. The result was unexpected. The first reason for the failure was, of course, that the defense was far inferior to that of the Pirates. Under the strict supervision of the opponent, they still attacked the basket, so they ran into walls everywhere. After entering, they also tried a few long shots, but they were inaccurate. Center Locke was guarded by Pirates' Center Ryan and had no chance of survival. He never hit a single shot. In terms of various techniques, they were not as experienced as the Pirates in this area.

A Glimpse of the Pirates' Performance

Compared to McLaren, the Pirates' performance was much better. Most of the time, the ball was in front of McLaren's basket. Carlson was in the middle, Smith and Squier flanked on both sides, and long men and Pyley were behind. This method was repeatedly effective. Carlson's backhand shot in the crowd hit many times, which was wonderful to watch. Squier's ability to penetrate was even more impressive. His power was undiminished. The long man caught the falling ball under the basket without a single mistake. It is a pity that Smith's shot was greatly reduced, otherwise the Pirates would have won long ago.

McLaren Follows Closely

Pirates' Squier scored the first goal, opening the record with two points. Byers hit one of his penalty shots, taking the lead 3 to 2. Both sides were very cautious. The Pirates took the lead again 6 to 4. Due to many penalties, McLaren took the lead twice 8 to 7. With one hit from Carlson, the Pirates gave up on following McLaren and took the lead all the way. After 16 to 9, McLaren worked harder to chase to 16 to 15 in the first half. The Pirates were only one point ahead.

The Pirates Finally Win

In the second half, the two sides were deadlocked for five or six minutes, and the Pirates were only able to gain one more point, and were once able to tie at 21. After 25 to 21, McLaren chased up two points, making it 25 to 23. Unexpectedly, McLaren stopped scoring from then on, and the Pirates succeeded everywhere. After one hit and then another, McLaren's mind was in a panic, and they were busy adjusting their troops, knowing that they were no longer able to compete. At 31 to 23, Byers was penalized, and McLaren declared despair. The final score was 36 to 25.
