Special Article

Ministry of Education Commissioner Going to Europe to Study Education

Vocational Education Report (10)

National Agricultural School: This school is a practical agricultural school. Admission requires an entrance examination, and the academic program is two years (except for the National School of Arts and Crafts in Versailles, which requires three years). It focuses on training farm work and management personnel. It is also a place where national colleges study practical experience.

Agricultural Schools: These types of schools are mostly established by provinces or cities, and sometimes by the state. The salaries of teachers are all paid by the state. The length of the academic program, admission qualifications, and curriculum standards vary greatly. They are determined by the Ministry of Agriculture according to local conditions or based on the recommendations of the school's management committee. All of the above three types of schools collect tuition and other fees, but they also provide scholarships and free places.

Winter Agricultural Schools: These types of schools are established for the children of farmers who cannot afford to attend ordinary schools. They are mostly attached to agricultural schools, middle schools, higher primary schools, or other public education institutions. Students must be at least fifteen years old, be the children of farmers, and have at least two years of farming experience.

Agricultural Extension Classes: Extension classes must be established at the request of the municipal government or the provincial agricultural education committee. Students must be at least thirteen years old, and the academic program is four years, with 150 hours of instruction each year. The teaching period is determined based on local conditions.

Women's Agricultural Education

Women's agricultural education is handled by the following schools: (1) National School of Domestic Science, (2) Agricultural School of Domestic Science (equivalent to agricultural schools), (3) Temporary Agricultural School of Domestic Science, similar in nature to winter schools, (4) Mobile Agricultural School of Domestic Science, (5) Agricultural and Domestic Science Extension Classes. Among the various types of women's agricultural education, the mobile agricultural school of domestic science is particularly distinctive. It is organized by each province and subsidized by the state. It travels to various cities and towns, providing rotational teaching. The locality must provide housing, water, and electricity, and all teaching materials related to rural domestic affairs, such as cooking, ironing, sewing, hat making, milk work, and livestock raising, must be carried by the teachers. The curriculum emphasizes both theory and practice. Graduates must pass an examination and are given diplomas.

Vocational Schools: Vocational schools are roughly divided into two categories: (1) Industrial and Commercial Practical Schools (or simply Practical Schools) and (2) Craft Schools.

Practical Schools: Those with a primary school diploma may enter at the age of twelve. Those without a diploma must be at least thirteen years old to enter. Needy children who have excellent grades may be given scholarships by the state, provincial government, or local government. The academic program of practical schools is three years, but most schools have a preparatory class for one year to allow students to acquire introductory skills in various crafts during this preparatory period to make a decision about their lifelong employment. In the first two years of practical school, the training courses are not divided into departments. However, in the third year of the regular class, students who wish to advance to higher vocational schools or specialize in a certain industry are given separate training. The so-called industrial or commercial certificate is also awarded at the end of the third year of the regular class. In addition to basic machine repair, tool making, and metalworking, practical school subjects include various specialties. In women's practical schools, domestic science is considered particularly important. Household management is considered the most important duty of women in France. The past achievements of practical schools are well known, and factories and shops are happy to employ their graduates. Each year, industrial and commercial certificate examinations are held, and practical school graduates must compete with apprentices from factories and shops. The subjects tested are biased towards practical experience, and the examiners are all employers, foremen, and shop assistants. However, the results of the examinations show that practical school students are often among the top ranks. Practical schools are either municipal or provincial. All routine maintenance costs, such as school building equipment and installations, are provided by the province or locality, and teacher salaries, except for the salaries of factory internship trainers, which are borne half by the locality or province, are all provided by the state's political expenses.

When a school is founded, the government provides a subsidy of 50% for both construction and equipment costs. This is stipulated by a 1923 decree. However, if a locality has donated a school building site, it may also be considered as part of the founding costs, but in this case, the national subsidy is also limited to providing for the full construction and equipment costs.

Craft Schools: Practical schools that specialize in training in a certain craft or industry are called craft schools, or they are prefixed with the name of the industry, such as shoe-making craft school, garment-making craft school, masonry craft school, plumbing craft school, hotel service craft school, etc. The organization of craft schools is very similar to that of practical schools. Representatives of the industry (employers or artisans, employees) are important members of the school's "improvement committee," but they are not permanent positions, so that the members of the committee will advance with the times and seek progress for the school. Rural areas have specialized craft schools that train rural artisans and rural workers to be familiar with machinery or electrical appliances used in agriculture. Currently, there are approximately 220 practical schools and craft schools throughout France, with approximately 30,000 students.

Factory Apprentice Training

Supplementary Classes: If factories and shops do not establish special schools to teach apprentices, then the training that young workers or employees receive will necessarily be limited to practical skills and lack general knowledge education and artistic theory. This type of training cannot be considered complete apprentice training, so the establishment of supplementary classes is an important driving force for vocational education.

Free Talk

On "Silence"

— Yu Dafu

Spontaneous silence, both in China and abroad, is regarded as a virtue in life. The Chinese say: "Calamity comes from the mouth!" So the wise keep their mouths shut. The British Carlyle said: "Silence and mystery! If this era were still an era of building altars, then the altars should be dedicated to them." He also quoted a Swiss proverb, "Speech is silver, silence is gold," and modified it to say: "Speech is temporary, silence is permanent." The Belgian symbolist Maeterlinck, in his essay collection "The Treasure of the Humble," praises silence to the highest degree.

He even says that the communication of souls through language is far less thorough than through silence. Especially when two people are in love, what determines this love is the first silence between them. When returning home from afar, when separation is imminent, when great joy is about to happen, when life ends, or when great misfortune is about to come, silence always precedes us. Therefore, what people fear most when there are many people is a deathly silence. The seriousness of silence is the seriousness of love, death, and fate.

Maeterlinck's praise of silence naturally has its own insights; but non-spontaneous silence is a bit uncomfortable. Let me tell you a story: Ji Xiaolan, the god of fire, was very fond of tobacco. One day, while he was puffing smoke and revising the Complete Library of the Four Treasuries, he suddenly heard a report: "The Emperor is here!" He stuffed his pipe into his boot and hurried down to greet the Emperor. Later, the fire burned his socks and flesh, and the smell of burning was coming out. The Emperor asked: "What's burning?" He just pretended to smile wryly and calmly replied: "Nothing!" This kind of silence really echoes the French saying that speech is the art of concealing thought. But although the art was successful, the flesh inevitably suffered pain.

Talking About Faces

— Ye Zi

A story circulating among the people of Shaoxing says that Bao Longtu and Di Qing swapped heads. Originally, Bao Gong was the literary star in the sky, and Di Qing was the military star. They descended to earth at the same time to support the Song Dynasty. Bao Gong was to be a civil official and should have had a fair face, while Di Qing was dark-headed, just like a military general. But when Bao Gong descended to earth, he mistakenly took Di Qing's head in haste, so Di Qing had to make do with wearing Bao Gong's head to descend to earth. Therefore, when Di Qing went to battle, he had to let his hair down and wear a copper mask to cover his fair face to make his appearance seem more awe-inspiring. And Bao Gong is still called "Bao Heitou" (Black Head).

It is hard to say who benefited from this transaction. If it was for building up strength, then Bao Gong would regret it, but in terms of career, a fair face was not only not good for Di Qing, but also reduced his prestige, so it can be seen that Di Qing was at a disadvantage. Bao Gong was different. He seems to have earned the reputation of "Yanluo" (King of Hell) largely due to his black head. Even his smile earned the beautiful name of "Yellow River Clearing," which shows that an ugly face was actually very valuable to him. It seems appropriate for someone who is a "law-enforcing and impartial" hard-nosed official to have such a face. In this case, Bao Gong benefited. Just from the point of view of not having to wear a mask, he was much more comfortable than Di Qing. So I suspect that Bao Gong's taking the wrong head may have been intentional.

Since the invention of firearms, the way of fighting has changed greatly. Today's military generals mostly stay in the rear and do not need to show their faces to intimidate the enemy. So it does not matter if they have a fair face, and there is no need to wear a copper mask. And having a fair face is very helpful in winning the hearts of women.

Memories in Sickness

— Liu Ming

When I was sick, I thought about going somewhere to have fun, but after thinking about it, there was no place to have fun. Like the grass in the park, I could sit on it, and the shady paths, I could walk on them. However, not having the money to buy a ticket to enter was a minor matter; if I didn't wear a gentleman's suit and put on a gentleman's face, going in would only increase my illness.

So, I had to sit in the room and meditate, replaying the most glorious scenes in my past life, one by one. Because, I felt, this should also be a plaything to make myself happy, right?

So, I walked into the park. Ah, a sea of plum blossoms, spreading fragrance. The winter sun, warmly smiling on the branches. Dewdrops and flower shadows, along the path, dripping on my clothes. Happiness flew out of my body. I forgot that I was still in this cursed Shanghai, and my body and mind had flown to my second hometown, Yunnan, which was far away in the clouds.

At that time, I was working as a handyman in the Kunming Red Cross Society, being scolded and bossed around all day long... I couldn't breathe freely under those heavy pressures.

Was it because I was sick that I got a vacation? Or was it due to something else? Anyway, I got a day off. Early in the morning, I sneaked to the park outside the South Gate, and while walking enthusiastically in the warm morning sun and among the sparse shadows of the plum blossoms, I looked at the vast and beautiful blue sky in the distance and whispered repeatedly:

"I am free! I am free!"

Happiness and joy, like invisible soap bubbles, evaporated from the cells of my whole body, flying one by one to the branches, to the grass, and up to the blue sky.

But, soon, acquaintances came, my masters came – they were either members of the Red Cross Society or directors, in short, all the richest people in the city.

Although they didn't say, "You, a handyman, are here too? Get out of here," I immediately felt uneasy and agitated, and even my breathing became hurried.

So, I lowered my head and fled the park.

All the way, I thought sadly: "Without equality in life, there is no freedom."

Haven't the black slaves in America been liberated for many years? But why are they still crying out to this day? I understood.

Recalling this, the glorious film shattered and disappeared.

There were no plum blossoms, no morning sun, all of life was dim, both past and present.

Go to bed and sleep! In this sick Shanghai.

Graduation Thesis

— Ye Chai

One

"How much?"

"Five dollars."

I shook my head:

"I won't do a graduation thesis for five dollars."

"Just so-so, Old Li – just randomly put something together, as long as it's an essay."

Old Hu frowned, looking very embarrassed. I perked up a little:

"Then, how many words do I need to write?"

"It has to be five or six thousand words, right?"

"Five or six thousand words?"

I glared at Old Hu. I shouted angrily in my heart:

"What? You want me to write six thousand words for five dollars! Is my writing not even worth one dollar per thousand words? Outrageous! I won't do it..."

"Help me out, Old Li! You're free anyway."

I, I, really can't do it…"

Old Hu looked like he was about to cry.

"Stupid thing! Who told you to come to me! You're not even a graduate?"

"I have no choice. This, is, is…"

"Whose is it?"

"Is, is…"

Old Hu hesitated embarrassedly. Then: "It's Miss Wang's!"

"Haha! You rascal! So you have a crush on Miss Wang! Fine, I'll help you out! Come and get it at lunchtime tomorrow. But, you have to give me the money first – my goods are cash only, no credit."

Old Hu happily left, and I borrowed three or four books on art overnight, copying a paragraph here, piecing together a few sentences there, until dawn, when I finally finished this great graduation thesis.

At noon, Old Hu ran over and took the essay without even looking at it. So I bought some wine and dishes and had a big feast in my garret.

Two

I was dreaming when someone ran into my garret.

"Why are you sleeping so early?"

"Ah, Miss Wang…"

I scrambled to my feet in a panic, feeling like I had been caught stealing: "Maybe my thesis is no good, and she's here to ask for a refund." I quickly greeted her with a smile:

"Please sit down! Long time no see!…"

I pretended to be very calm.

"Yes! I've been really busy. I, cough! Cough! … Here!…"

She took out a stack of manuscript paper from her bosom and placed it on the table. Then:

"It's all because of this graduation thesis! I've been working myself to death, looking for reference books for over a week to finish it. Now, please give me…"

"Ah!…"

I almost laughed my teeth off. Then, I said respectfully:

"I dare not! I dare not! It must be very good."

"Please correct it, please correct it!…"

So I opened the package of paper:

My scribbled mess had been copied over by her. At the beginning: Not bad. Looking down: Not bad. Two words were missing: It doesn't matter. A sentence was changed: Hmm! Changed for the worse… So-so. Another sentence was changed: Hmm! … I had to keep looking with a heavy heart, finally… Heavens! I couldn't bear it any longer:

"Miss Wang! Good! Good! But, I feel…" I stammered:

"I feel, this, this place… it seems…"

"Oh! Yes! This place…"

"It doesn't quite fit, does it?…"

"Oh! So! Oh! … Then, please…" I quickly grabbed a pen and scribbled all over it, replacing it with my original text. She stood beside me, looking very embarrassed: "Thank you! I was simply confused by the reference books!"

Correction

Editor:

In the 21st's "Free Talk" article, in the third paragraph of "Critic of Critics", the last line, "He has no fixed circle" should be "He must have a fixed circle". Please correct it. Thank you. Ni Shuoer.

Father and Daughter (5)

— Jin Yi

"You didn't think about your daughter!"

Her eyes stared at the empty wall, her tone like that of an old woman who had completely despaired of the world.

He still didn't speak, sometimes raising his palms to his eyes, as if looking at the patterns on them; but his eyes were filled with tears, and he couldn't see anything clearly. He only knew that the person sitting by the bed was his daughter, the daughter who had sacrificed her life for him, she had cried, had cried sadly for him. He knew he loved her, she was such a lovable child. He also knew that he still loved her now, but he had made her cry. He understood the reason, had nothing to say, he wanted his daughter to blame him, even to scold him, he could bear it. He saw the wine bottles lying on the ground, his regret overwhelmed him like the entire sky pressing on his heart. He wanted to stand up and smash them with his feet; but he thought that it would be useless, so he restrained himself again. His mouth was dry, needing some water to moisten it, he knew he didn't have the strength to stand up, nor could he ask his daughter, although he knew she wouldn't refuse him. He endured it, and when he couldn't bear it any longer, his mouth made a sound, his tongue licking his upper palate. She saw it, stood up, took a teacup from the cupboard, and poured a full cup from the thermos. She walked over and offered it to his hands; but seeing his trembling hands, she didn't hand it over, but sat on the ground next to the chair and brought the teacup to his mouth. He looked at her face, the face that still had traces of tears, and lowered his head to drink the water. He drank the entire cup in one breath. She asked softly:

"Do you want more?"

He tilted his head slightly and shook it, but two large teardrops were embedded in the corners of his eyes again. She didn't bother to put down the teacup in her hand, but leaned over him and began to cry. Her tears soaked through his clothes, warmly as if warming his heart, and he stroked her body with his hands.

"Child… you are right to complain about me…"

He used a lot of strength to say this sentence, he had many more words to say; but it was as if something had choked his throat, and he couldn't say anything more. He could only let his tears wash his face like water.

"You don't know these days…" he forced himself to continue, "these days my heart is so painful… that dark shadow is cast upon me… only making me sad. Last night… there was such a good moon… child, you don't know…"

He paused, wiping the tears from his face with his hand.

"Your mother and I confessed our love to each other under such a good moonlight… the moonlight was so good… when I kissed her forehead… I could see… I could see her hair, strand by strand. Last night's moon was naturally not as good as that… but I thought… this moonlight is also shining on her… so I became happy. Do you understand, my happiness brought even greater melancholy… I don't know where she is… I don't know if she is also thinking of me?"

He paused again, she knew the reason for this pause, but she still asked: "Dad, would you like some more water?"

He nodded, but when she brought him a cup of water, he only drank one sip and asked her to put it aside. She gently rubbed her eyes, still sitting beside him. He continued to say: "I know she won't be thinking of me… if she thought of me, she could come to me… but I am stupid, many people say that about me… you may also say that about me… but I can't forget her. Last night I was thinking of her even more deeply… I almost couldn't live without seeing her face immediately. I had no choice, child… so I quietly took out the wine you had sealed for me." His voice became dry. "I didn't forget you… I remembered that I had promised you never to let wine touch my lips again… but the thought of her tormented me so much… that I had to immerse myself in wine to forget her… that's how it was, I wanted to forget her. But, after one bottle was already drunk, her shadow flashed more clearly in my mind… so, I opened another bottle. This made me drunk, so drunk that I didn't know anything… I forgot her, I forgot everything. I slept on the ground like a shameless drunkard… this ugly appearance made my beloved daughter cry for me, I am just a fool… I am not worthy to be your father!"

In the end, he cried out loud, and slumped down again. He hid his face in his hands as if feeling ashamed, but his daughter comforted him with a gentle voice: "Don't be sad, Dad, I'm just worried about your health. I know you love me, I don't want you to continue like this…"

Commercial News

Significant Rise in Gold Standard Prices

Sharp Increase of Six Yuan and Seventy Cents Due to Covering Short Positions

Since the gold market stabilized recently, the underlying trend has been bullish. Yesterday, the market suddenly strengthened, and the upward momentum was quite strong. In the morning, the overseas silver market saw no change in both the U.S. and the U.K. The forward silver price at the Five Metals Exchange rose by 1.4 and 3.1 fen, respectively. Exchange rate fluctuations were small. The London gold price rose by two pence, stocks fell by 4.3 jiao, U.S. wheat fell by 0.875, U.S. cotton fell by 9 pounds, and the opening price of the wool market retreated to 88-89 yuan, indicating a weak trend. Reuters reported that U.S. Senator Teller advocated proposing a currency amendment to restore silver coinage. However, Teller and King's meeting with the President yielded little result. Therefore, the market opened weakly but remained flat, with continued narrow fluctuations. Later, Sassoon & Co. came in to buy shillings and U.S. dollars. Despite the news of the U.S. Senate passing a rural public debt of $2,000,000,000, the gold market was very bullish, breaking through the 90 yuan mark. The market opened steadily afterward, indicating that major players had already covered their short positions, and market confidence strengthened. Subsequently, Chinese merchants covered their short positions, and the Central Exchange Bureau continued to buy aggressively, tightening the foreign exchange market. HSBC's exchange rate quotation was further reduced, and the gold price rapidly rebounded. The highest price reached 1,090 yuan. Below is a record of the day's market conditions:

The opening price in the morning was 687.3 yuan, down 4 yuan from the previous close. The item price opened at 7.2 jiao. The opening exchange rate was 1 shilling 4.4375 pence for recent sales of British currency and 34.3125 yuan for U.S. currency. Sumitomo accepted May U.S. dollars at 0.875. Hengyu, Yongfeng, Hengtai, Chunyuan, and Yong accepted terms, and rose to 8.5 yuan. Yuanmao, Yongyi, and Dayong sold terms, retreating to 7.5 yuan. However, because Pangen accepted May U.S. dollars at 0.875, HSBC's quotation revealed a flat British currency and an increase of 0.125 for U.S. currency, the situation was still stable. Zhengjin ate June U.S. dollars at 35.0625 yuan. Shunli, Fuyu, Zhaofeng, and Changjin reached 8.5 yuan. Hengxing continued to supply, once falling, but because Ruikang limited purchases, the gold market continued to stabilize. Later, Hengxing, Zhengchang, and Dadecheng suddenly advanced, Hengchang sold and then advanced again, rising to 9 yuan. Silk and Tea: Difficulty in Turning Around Overseas Silk Sales

Last Year's Surge in Russian Silk Exports to the US: In recent years, the Soviet Union has actively developed its sericulture industry, sending personnel to silk-producing countries such as Japan and Italy to purchase silkworm eggs and mulberry saplings, and rewarding farmers for raising silkworms and planting mulberry trees. Both silkworm egg production and silk production have increased year by year. The silk produced is mainly sold in the United States. Last year saw a surge in Russian silk exports to the US. According to a telegram received by American silk merchants in this port from the New York Silk Association, the total amount of Russian silk exported to the US last year reached 5,797 bales (based on Kilo Chehe).

Factory-Woven Silk Sales are Not Lively: In the overseas raw silk market, due to reduced production by factories and other facilities, the consumption of raw silk has not increased. Furthermore, the old prices of Japanese silk remain stable, and sales of Chinese silk factory products remain sluggish, with telegrams indicating a downturn. European merchants are taking a wait-and-see attitude. Only the inland silk market is still active, and although market prices have risen by more than twenty yuan, factories still have to incur losses. Yesterday, another 50 bales of yellow and white factory-woven silk were traded, and 20 bales of French grey silk were imported, with prices remaining firm.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Random Remarks

The Temporality of Cigarettes

— Fei Ren

Every day, I come out from my small apartment and go to the school to teach. I pass through a very bustling place, and in the middle of this place, there is an extremely large wall. This wall is the most suitable place for shop advertisements.

The first advertisement I discovered on this wall was for Ma Zhanshan cigarettes. At that time, the painting on the wall was of a national hero, riding a horse and waving a flag, with imposing demeanor. This was during the period of national salvation and resistance against Japan, fully expressing the spirit of a national hero. Before long, the advertisement disappeared.

What I continued to discover in this place was an advertisement for Butterfly brand cigarettes. The painting on the wall was of a graceful woman, charming and elegant, making one feel like ascending to immortality, with one's soul flying away for half a day. This clearly indicated that the work of national salvation was already completed, and this was the period of entertainment. Before long, the advertisement disappeared again.

What arose in response to the times was the Meng Jiangnv cigarette advertisement. Meng Jiangnv traveled thousands of miles in search of her husband. Isn't she the most pitiful and sympathetic woman in history? This clearly expresses the meaning of sorrow arising from extreme joy. When I thought of this, I thought everyone should wake up, but by this time, it was too late to wake up.

I see that these three advertisements have a definite continuity and are very sufficient to represent the attitudes of our people in three periods.

Ah! Meng Jiangnv, when will you finally find your husband?

Women's Year of National Products: Introspection

— Xiu

Yesterday morning (January 21st), I unfolded a copy of the "Old Newspaper That's Not Old" Shen Bao, and I was shocked to see on it the heartbreaking statistic: "Last year's foreign trade deficit exceeded 410 million yuan." I think that creating such a huge trade deficit for foreign merchants in trade with China must be attributed to the enthusiasm of the compatriots who love to use foreign goods, especially the enthusiastic and tireless promotion by the sisters in the women's circle!

But in the past year, which was called the "Year of National Products," the amount of the trade deficit has been so huge. Isn't this too much of a joke! How can we Chinese people, who usually sing the praises of "promoting national products" so loudly, explain ourselves?

While I was looking at this newspaper and filled with emotion, our little statistician, Xuemei, came. She had compiled statistics on the new films shown in Shanghai's theaters last year, totaling 427, of which foreign films accounted for 355 and domestic films only 73. We call her "Little Statistician" because she likes to make these kinds of statistical tables. I pointed to this record of the trade deficit and sighed to her: "Please, you statistician, go and calculate how much of this trade deficit of 411,784,900 yuan comes from the outflow of money from our hands?"

She replied with a bitter smile, "Naturally, the majority is spent by our female compatriots, and the most enthusiastic promoters of this huge leakage are the modern women. In addition to the clothes on their bodies, the precious jewelry and diamond rings on their hands, etc., the cost of cosmetics such as silk stockings, high heels, and perfumes is also quite considerable. Didn't Miss Huang tell you? She spends more than 80 yuan a year buying Paris lipsticks for a little bit of cherry lips!"

After hearing her words, I couldn't help but nod my head in agreement, saying, "That's right, not only those extravagant and luxurious wives and young ladies often flaunt the use of expensive foreign goods, but even we cannot avoid spending white and shiny silver to buy foreign goods. Look at the fountain pens and inkwells in front of us, they are genuine imported goods! Alas! 'What's past cannot be corrected, but what's to come can still be pursued.' Since this year is the Women's Year of National Products, we must introspect ourselves more carefully in the future, and even for a single needle or thread, we must purchase national products..."

Before I finished speaking, she immediately stood up, expressing her determination, "Good! Let's resolve to do that. Even if we cannot suddenly turn such a huge trade deficit into a trade surplus, in any case, if we buy one less yuan of foreign goods, we can promote one more yuan of national products, and we can also reduce the trade deficit by one yuan and recover one yuan of rights and interests..."

Hearing her enthusiastic words, I couldn't help but clap my hands and shout "Good!", and I also learned a slogan and shouted loudly: "Female compatriots across the country, let us unite and work hard to promote national products and use national products as much as possible in this 'Women's Year of National Products'!"

Each Has Their Own World

— Lao Pai

It was one o'clock in the afternoon, and I struggled to drag my dizzy and heavy body out of bed.

Subconsciously, I walked out of the alley.

The wind was howling so fiercely that any water droplets on the ground had frozen into ice. Although the number of people coming and going was as large as usual, they were not as busy as weaving shuttles. It could be said that everyone was carrying their heads between their shoulders like filial sons at a funeral, just moving slowly.

The wind was howling so fiercely that everyone was afraid of the cold.

But here, there were:

Four dirty little girls. If they were a little taller, they would be old enough to start their careers of selling smiles and flesh in the "street corner" "warehouses" of the Fourth Avenue business district. Looking at them carefully, their faces were indeed fair. What they lacked was a body of clothes to protect themselves. But they were not completely naked either. Some were draped in burlap sacks, some seemed to be wearing men's broken jackets, and some were wearing things that made it impossible to discern what they were. …

All four were shivering.

Yet, all four were rejoicing.

After a while of "gossiping," they all kicked shuttlecocks together.

After a change of pace, they took turns jumping rope.

Smiles filled each of their dirty faces, showing their joy for life, their satisfaction with the reality of life, without disgust or evil thoughts.

But I think their lives are precarious enough, and in reality, they are not allowed to be so joyful.

Because of this, for a while, I couldn't find an answer.

It wasn't until I was having dinner that evening, when Peng suggested going to a restaurant, but I only wanted to spend two dimes to buy some beef to cook myself, that the question stuck in my mind was dissected in an instant.

It turned out that I was the same as those four dirty little girls—I always expressed joy for life, satisfaction with the reality of life, without disgust or evil thoughts.

I had never thought about "becoming an official," and I had never thought about "getting rich," so I was very ignorant of how many "official positions" there were in the small city of Shanghai, and I didn't know what issue the aviation lottery tickets had been issued to. I only knew to work on time every day, eat, laugh, … smoke cigarettes and other things. Although sometimes I also wanted to find something suitable to do, I wasn't in a hurry to pursue it, thinking that I could get by as long as I could make a living, so why be so busy and so serious?

Naturally, there are many people like this. Among the 400 million compatriots, there are not only the four dirty little girls and me.

Our ancient sages' maxims say, "Be content and guard your position," "Be content with fate and enjoy life," "Wealth and honor are determined by fate." In short, it is "fatalism." All things, the arrangement of life, the success or failure of the future, are all left to the word "fate." There is no need to think too much or work hard.

In this way, of course, everyone is very well-behaved. Someone tells you to sit down, and you sit down, saying that sitting down is good. Someone tells you to stand up, and you stand up, saying that standing up is even better.

As for whether the "nation" and "society" have therefore become old and unprogressive, that is somewhat obscure to say and can only be left unspecified.

Talking About A Destiny of Tears and Laughter

—

I didn't read A Destiny of Tears and Laughter when it was serialized daily in the Kuaihuolin section of the Xinwen Bao. I didn't read A Destiny of Tears and Laughter when it was applauded and cheered in the local supplement. I didn't read A Destiny of Tears and Laughter when Zhang Shichuan and Gu Wuwei were scheming and fighting each other. I didn't read A Destiny of Tears and Laughter when Wang Meiyu played two roles at the same time. I didn't read A Destiny of Tears and Laughter when Xue Xiaoqing and Zhu Yaoxiang were engaged in a war of words. I didn't read A Destiny of Tears and Laughter when the Sanyou Bookstore offered a reward for illegal printing. I didn't read A Destiny of Tears and Laughter in... I didn't read it. So how can you talk about A Destiny of Tears and Laughter? (I also want to ask), here it comes, on New Year's Day in 1934, I returned home for two days and found this well-known novel in my cousin's bookshelf. My cousin is a current university student, and A Destiny of Tears and Laughter also occupies a place among the many books and social science books piled up. So I finished this giant work with a beautiful head drawn on the cover in two sleepless nights. However, the image it gave me was so vague that my talk about A Destiny of Tears and Laughter is nothing more than a boring thing.

The four ideal characters in A Destiny of Tears and Laughter｜｜Fan Jashu, Shen Fengxi, Guan Xiugu, and He Lina, are as easily deeply imprinted into the minds of grandmothers and young ladies as Tang Bohu and Qiuxiang. Having grown accustomed to old tunes such as The Story of the Three Smiles and The Pearl Pagoda, when the general petite bourgeoisie were pursuing new forms of escapism, A Destiny of Tears and Laughter was destined to be born at this time. Its overnight popularity was as unsurprising as a winter sale.

Fan Jashu is essentially a typical petit bourgeois. He left his hometown and came to this ancient city of Beijing, where there is no wind three feet above the ground and mud on the streets after rain, for the sake of studying. However, when I read to the last page of Candlelight in Pairs, it seemed that there was not a single line that told me that Fan Jashu was a university student seeking intellectual satisfaction, or because the image it gave me was too vague, it slipped past my eyes when I wasn't paying attention. Since A Destiny of Tears and Laughter has been published in its third edition, among the many readers at the end, there will always be—as long as they read it word for word, this question can probably be resolved.

Since Fan Jashu's stunning appearance at Tianqiao (a phrase stolen from The Romance of the Western Chamber｜｜self-note by Dai Ni) and his encounters with Guan Xiugu and He Lina, he has been circulating among three different types of women. I thought it would definitely be a grand comedy like Nine Beauties Reunion. However, Shen Fengxi went crazy, Guan Xiugu drifted away and disappeared, and our petit bourgeois Fan Jashu finally married Miss He, a suitable match. The author also stated at the end of the book that he could not attribute all three beauties to Fan Jashu (forgive me for not being able to quote the original sentence from the book), which seemed to be beyond my expectation. However, readers should know that Qiuxiang in The Story of the Three Smiles is essentially a young lady, and will be the adopted daughter of Hua Taishi in the future; therefore, marrying Tang Yin, a top scholar, is equivalent to the perfect match between Fan Jashu and He Lina, which is a major ending that follows the will of heaven. The daughter who sings drums and sells solutions can never turn over the palm of the Buddha. In this way, it seems that it is not beyond our expectations.

I don't want to say anything more about these four main characters, because I wasn't careful enough when I read the book, and I don't have a copy of A Destiny of Tears and Laughter on hand now.

My grandmother read Li Hanzhu's Mirror Image of People, and said that his writing was "penetrating". Now A Destiny of Tears and Laughter also suffers from this common problem. At least I think it is too idealized. Although we don't have to cite the characters in the book to our surroundings, I have heard that A Destiny of Tears and Laughter is indeed a real event, so the exaggeration of the description will naturally lose its authenticity, because I did not experience that it was a "real event" when I read A Destiny of Tears and Laughter. Although my current university student cousin said that she shed tears of sympathy, just like when she read Jade Pear Soul.

Referring again to Mr. Hen Shui's writing of each character's personality, they are all so strong. Now that he is writing seven or eight novels at the same time, I wonder if he still maintains his original style? I can also be sure that he is a movie fan. He is very good at using small actions, but unlike movies, he often adds unnecessary details (can these four words be used?) after the small actions to state that these are "small actions." In the entire book A Destiny of Tears and Laughter, I really want to use Cut's surgery to dig a few trenches. You see, in the end, he still uses circled lead letters to satisfy a reader's question. I think if every reader had a letter of questioning, A Destiny of Tears and Laughter could at least double in length.

This giant work of A Destiny of Tears and Laughter, which I finished in two sleepless nights, can no longer be "talked about," so I admit that it is nothing more than a boring thing: but I hope that there will be others who are more boring than me after reading my "Talking About A Destiny of Tears and Laughter."

Finally, apply the old method and drag a tail: The part about Guan Shoufeng's night visit to the general's mansion can be read as a martial arts novel.

Selling One's Life

— Lüdí

In today's society of the survival of the fittest, the cry of unemployment is as common as raising one's head to look at the sky, so it is no longer surprising. University students are spending sleepless years, and officials have to offer their daughters first. Naturally, if one is lucky enough to grab a job through auction, one must bow and scrape and shorten one's own life, or one's job is always in the dangerous time of "sand crabs"; so how can writers who rack their brains not sigh!

These cruel facts are being performed continuously before our eyes every day, as long as you pay a little attention to your surroundings. However, the most important condition is that your own job is also in suspense; otherwise, you are merely adding to the after-dinner conversation regarding this type of performance.

The performer Sun Debao acted with all her might, selling her life, these few number two characters jumped into my eyes. This at least basic performer, Sun Debao, does not have the "world fame" of Mei Lanfang. She performs in the Tianyunlou Fenghang class, just like we basic writers write articles in the butt of newspapers. She cannot make a splash on the red carpet for a month, rest for a year and a half, and then be rehired with heavy money, and "rest for a few days and choose an auspicious day to take the stage again." She "sells her life" every day, using low-level "skills" to win the applause of the audience under the stage, so she even tries Somersault kicks, holding onto that job that is always in danger of "sand crabs"; but "luck ran out for too long, and she collapsed on the ground from shortness of breath," "selling her life and returning to heaven."

I myself did not "cheer" at this event. I wonder what the audience, who spent two dimes to enjoy low-level interests, felt when they returned home and enjoyed a steaming hot dinner? In so-called Shanghai, it is difficult to hear one or two sighs of regret that a weak flesh was swallowed effortlessly by the strong; however, how can writers who rack their brains not sigh! Alas, Sun Debao!

Amateur Mailbox

Learning Specialized Skills to Avoid Unemployment

Editor:

I am an unfortunate person who entered a store at the age of fifteen and began living as an apprentice. I have not received any new education, only reading the Analects and Mencius for six or seven years. I have been in the business world for five years now. I have been unemployed three times in these five years. Working or seeking work in old-fashioned small and medium-sized stores almost always depends on connections; whether you have the ability is secondary. Let's talk about ability. It's just writing and arithmetic. This is the most common skill. I think that among the unemployed, there must be many who have this skill. So I believe that my personal method of struggle is to desperately seek a practical specialized knowledge to overcome the harsh environment. Now it is possible to study during the day, but the following questions have arisen:

(1) I am now nineteen years old, so I hope to obtain a specialized knowledge within three or four years, but my level is only equivalent to junior high school in Chinese, and I have studied English arithmetic for half a year in night school and know addition, subtraction, multiplication, and division. I have no other knowledge. I am determined to study industry, but without a junior high school qualification, I cannot enter a higher vocational school, let alone a technical college. Sir, what method can you guide me to create a junior high school qualification in the shortest period of time and seek the knowledge I want to seek?

(2) Studying industry requires a longer period of study. If, due to time and economic reasons, I cannot achieve my ambition, then I think I will have to study wireless telegraphy. I heard that there is a wireless radio school established by the Ministry of Transportation in Shanghai. What is the name of the school? After graduating from the school, can the Ministry of Transportation assign me to work or intern at various radio stations? Please give me an answer.

(3) You may understand half of the environment I am in from this letter. If the methods I said before are not appropriate, sir, can you point out another way out for me?

Hu Hezhong Qi

Editor's note: Regarding the three points you asked, here are the answers:

(1) Recently, schools have paid a lot of attention to qualifications when enrolling students. You have not received school education, so it seems difficult to enter school. It is very difficult to "create a junior high school qualification in the shortest period of time" because you already have a job and cannot go back to school, and there is no preparatory school equivalent to junior high school yet.

(2) There is indeed a telegraph school established by the Ministry of Transportation. I heard that it is divided into wireless and wired classes. However, it is said that the entrance examination is very strict, and it is very difficult to pass the exam with your level. It is not clear whether you will be assigned a job in the future.

(3) You are now planning to obtain specialized knowledge to avoid unemployment. This view is not entirely correct. It must be known that unemployment in society is not caused by the unemployed lacking work skills, but is a phenomenon that is inevitably produced by the current society. You have also felt this: knowing that the unemployed are not without skills; however, you think that having specialized knowledge will make you not worry about unemployment, but that is not necessarily the case. There are still many people with specialized work skills who are unemployed, because occupations are also the same as commodities and are determined by the relationship between supply and demand; if the society is steadily improving, and production undertakings are extremely developed, and many people are needed to do things, then people with work skills can not worry about unemployment, because there are very few talents like this with work skills, and the society needs these people to do things. On the contrary, if the social production undertakings are not very developed, then even if you have the skills of a heavenly dog, you will not be able to do anything, because at this time the society does not feel a "talent shortage," but people feel a "job shortage"! Therefore, your hope to solve the employment problem by acquiring specialized knowledge is not a very reliable method, because in China today, the lack of "other material conditions for developing production" is the main reason why industry cannot develop, and the "lack of talents with production skills" is still secondary, but from an individual point of view, what other methods are there besides hoping to increase work skills, even though this is not a reliable method. According to your situation, we think that it is best not to have any great ambitions for the time being and to learn some "specialized skills." It is best to honestly put some effort into the national language and read more books on common sense of social sciences. If your writing is fluent and your common sense is rich, then it may be more convenient to seek work, because doing things in society always takes the ability to write ordinary application texts as a prerequisite. As for the common sense of social sciences, it can help you understand the current society and know your position in the current society. In this way, even if you feel the shortcomings of various environments, you can also not "blame heaven and complain about others." At the same time, it can also enable you to have a little confidence in dealing with the social environment. Therefore, we believe that learning these two subjects is beneficial to you.

Fiction

The Freedom of Marilyn (5)

— Man Zhi

One day, it was a late autumn night, with a drizzle falling. He staggered out of a bar, completely drunk. The autumn wind on the street brought the alcohol rushing to his chest and brain, leaving him with no senses. He stumbled unconsciously down the road. A rickshaw stopped in front of the BAE entrance of a foreign bar. After a foreign sailor jumped out, he refused to pay. The rickshaw puller chased after him to demand payment. The foreign sailor kicked him, and the rickshaw puller fell to the ground. Through his drunken haze, Renjie vaguely saw this tragedy. Instinctively, he knew that the foreign sailor was bullying a poor Chinese man. His unique Northern chivalry, the inherent sense of justice, compelled him to immediately attack the foreign sailor, cursing him in English. Both were drunk, their strength amplified beyond normal. Both subconsciously understood that the foreign sailor was shouting, "You yellow-skinned Chinaman dare to fight us!" and he was shouting, "You foreign scoundrel, a butcher who won't ascend to heaven, you look down on everyone!" They cursed and grappled. Because he was wearing gentleman's clothes and speaking English, the Indian police showed him deference and didn't dare arrest him. Others, like the bar owner and the White Russian prostitutes, didn't dare help the foreign sailor. They wrestled for a long time. Eventually, the foreign sailor's strength waned, and he couldn't beat him, so he fled back into the bar. He returned home triumphantly, as excited as a national hero returning from victory.

However, he was injured! He was admitted to the hospital the next day.

In the hospital, his fever reached 105 degrees. During the day, he rambled in his sleep.

"That sailor, that foreign butcher, hit him, hit him, send him back home!"

"Marilyn, Marilyn, you're back? I beat up that foreign sailor."

"You don't approve? You say I was reckless? I was fighting imperialism!"

"Marilyn, Marilyn, why are you angry with me?…"

"Marilyn, darling, you can't leave me!"

"Marilyn, you have to understand me."

"Marilyn, Marilyn! You! You!…"

He went mad! He hit the nurse, cursing her as a foreign scoundrel. He jumped out of bed, hitting everyone, disrupting the order of the hospital.

Marilyn, the day he was admitted to the hospital, I sent you a telegram. Didn't you receive it? How could you bear not to come and see him? It's your fault!

Your fault is not understanding him. Don't argue. Although you understand his state of mind, you don't understand why he feels that way. That's why you don't understand him.

In this turbulent era, a young person with thoughts, a mind, and ambition must participate in political movements. Their keen senses feel the pulse of the oppressed people. They must run to the forefront of the times to do something beneficial for the country, society, and humanity. Once deceived by the environment, discouraged by indifferent companions, and faced with a bleak political future… all kinds of stimulation will inevitably lead to resentment and a search for numbness. This kind of disillusionment and sorrow of decline is given to him by the times, and it is also brought on by his own class destiny. Renjie is one of many such young people. You don't understand his kind of depression and distress because you lack political thought. Can you say it's his fault that he didn't teach you to understand?

Marilyn, you should recognize yourself. You are a woman who has fallen behind!

Film Supplement

The Rise of Nude Films (Part 1)

— Guangdao

The Trend That Was Seen in Advance

The United States Has Already Begun Preparing New Films

Everyone is asking now: "Will nude films, in the near future, become a trend, a recognized genre of film, like the 'Westerns' or 'Social Films' we already have?" Or: "Will young Mr. and Mrs. Smith be debating one evening in a year or two whether to take their children to a travel film or a nude film?" Please don't say it's impossible or won't happen. Because nude films have already appeared in America. Films of nude movements are already visible. The actors inside are all naked. And many more are already in production. Now almost every filmmaker is turning the idea over in their mind, thinking of ideas on how to apply the purpose of this newly emerging nude movement to shoot some timely films.

"Back to Nature" is the pioneer of nude films. It has already given American filmmakers in general an impression of a possible trend. When it is shown, the audience in the theater is packed to the brim. The second film, written by Bryan Foy, is "Elysia," which is more intimate and dramatic. Its attraction is even greater than "Back to Nature." This subject matter, in the midst of a lack of boring subjects, seems to have discovered a new field, making everyone feel endless excitement and stimulation.

The love story of a nude movement practitioner is bound to be fresher and more interesting than all the current "clothed films." Many filmmakers have already foreseen the near future and are thinking about what actors to use to shoot this new style of film. But how much longer will it be before they can discuss in meetings whether the Garbos or Dietrichs will shoot a film for winter, or wait until spring and shoot a "clothed" film first? Please don't laugh either, because this ideal will soon become a reality. If you don't believe it, look at Paramount's recent contract with Sally Rand. Sally Rand is a nude dancer at the Chicago World's Fair. Paramount, seeing her voluptuous figure, recruited her and gave her a contract of $5,000 a week. Although there is no talk of shooting nude films yet, Paramount's forward-looking approach clearly indicates the future direction of filmmaking.

According to reliable sources, Greta Garbo is very much in favor of this new movement. If there were an appropriate nude film script for her to do, she would definitely be willing to take off her clothes and perform, because she is originally a believer in nude sunbathing. In addition, there are many other stars who are already turning the idea over in their minds, considering this issue. Try closing your eyes and imagining Joan Crawford and Clark Gable as the two leads in a nude love film! Or Johnny Weissmuller and Jean Harlow! And the most surprising thing is that Mae West, with her voluptuous figure and overflowing charm, is a woman who opposes nude films. She says that taking off clothes is something everyone can do, but to truly achieve artistic touch that elevates the viewer's imagination to the clouds, one must wear clothes. Therefore, women must have appropriate clothing and know how to apply them before they can become popular. (To be continued)

Warner Brothers' Approach to the Blue Eagle Movement

— Anding

Since the Democratic Party's Roosevelt took office in the United States, Warner Brothers has been transformed into a Democratic propaganda machine in an invisible way. The art of film is now used by every country as a tool of education and propaganda. Socialist Soviet Union, Fascist Italy and Germany have all given full play to its role of propaganda and education. Capitalist America, of course, cannot be an exception, so since Roosevelt came to power, Warner Brothers has become a propaganda weapon in the Blue Eagle movement.

The second war of plunder among international powers is about to break out in an instant. The clever Roosevelt, he knows that the crisis of the Second World War is at hand, he knows that he will again drive millions of innocent people to the battlefield, to be the victims of their rulers, the ruling parties, the bankers, ×× kings... and so on. Therefore, he had no choice but to start a narcotic movement. At the same time, he could also take the opportunity to attack the opposition party - the Republican Party, to gain public sympathy and consolidate the power of the Democratic Party.

In 1933, under the command of the Democratic Party, Warner Brothers produced films on a large scale to promote Roosevelt's revival movement. For example, "Gold Diggers of 1933" and "42nd Street," which have been screened in Shanghai and take unemployed workers as their subject. Now there is another film on the subject of veteran soldiers, "Heroes For Sale" (this film: the Japanese translation is America's discussion of Russia), but according to the original text, it should be translated as: "Heroes for Sale" or "Heroes Priceless"). In the past, such American films, apart from entertainment and intoxication, had no other purpose, but now, it is very different. For example, "Gold Diggers of 1933" and "Heroes For Sale" have actually become the mouthpiece for propagating the Democratic Party's political program. Now that Warner Brothers has such a political background, its approach, of course, also "changes" with the overall situation.

Recently, there is a very important question in the United States, which is the "question of veterans." Warner Company of the Democratic Party, in order to win the sympathy of the people, used the slogan of "opposing the suspension of veterans' allowances," to produce the film "Wild Boys of the Road." The production of "Wild Boys of the Road" is based on these three principles:

(1) Opposing the suspension of veterans' allowances,

(2) The treatment of veterans,

(3) Relief movement for the unemployed. The content describes that in the spring of the previous year (February 1932), more than 20,000 veterans came to Washington, D.C., surrounded the White House, paraded and gave speeches, opposing the Republican Party's abandonment of support during its administration, and demanding that the government fulfill its obligations. However, that sensational demonstration was distorted by Warner Brothers. It simply insulted that heroic struggle and the more than 20,000 fighters.

Now the golden land of the New World is filled with cries of hunger. But can the Blue Eagle movement save the current America? Can the millions of "forgotten good people" - veterans and unemployed workers - who are oppressed by hunger and cold get bread from Roosevelt's hands?

Anna Sten's Coco Dance Bing

—

Russian star Anna Sten, since joining United Artists in Hollywood, has not been on camera for a long time because she is too fat. Now she will be starring in a new film, Gola's Nana. In this new film, she will be performing a special dance, called the "Coco" dance, Can Can dance, which has never been seen in any country. There are also two Coco dance songs, which she will also be singing. Now she is very capable of being on camera, she has reduced her weight from 150 pounds to 120 pounds, and is able to dance easily.

Anna Sten has a special skill, she can perform the expressions of many characters at the same time. Once, she performed fifty-one different people at United Artists, she can change her hair, and can change her voice, change her attitude, from a child to a mother. She is showing off this special skill in the Coco Dance.

Because Anna Sten is not good at speaking English, she is now behind the others. In fact, she has very good art. She used to star in four films, but she only said a few simple words. Now her English is very good. According to Maurice Sheffordstone, the manager of United Artists, his comment on her is that she will definitely be a promising figure in the film industry in the future.

Gary Cooper's Heartbreak

— Donglin

Many people think that a beautiful star like Gary Cooper enjoys all the pleasures of life, but the fact is completely the opposite, he often tastes the pain of heartbreak!

His first love was a classmate in college, named Therese. Gary left her in his hometown and ran to Hollywood to find his "luck." He finally got a chance to be a bit player in a martial arts film. During this time, because he was not diligent in corresponding with Therese, Therese thought he had abandoned her, so she married the village pharmacist.

He also had an affair with flapper girl Clara Bow. At that time, Clara Bow was already a famous star, and he was only a newcomer to the silver screen, so this matter was mostly initiated by the woman. But the frivolous Clara Bow would never be satisfied with the "country bumpkin" Gary forever, so their romance soon disappeared.

Later, he fell in love with the passionate Mexican girl Lupe Vélez. However, in less than a year, she ran away. Cooper went to Africa to hunt, also because of this heartbreak.

Shi Dongshan Writes "Woman"

— Waves

Starring Li Minghui and Hu Ping

Shi Dongshan's film "Woman" is about to start shooting. Because the script review committee was very satisfied with the script of "Woman," written by Shi Dongshan of Yihua Company, and at the same time, wrote these words on another page of the script: "This film is quite meaningful and close to worldly sentiment." Naturally, this is tantamount to giving many people in Yihua Company a shot of excitement.

Therefore, Shi Dongshan is preparing to make some slight modifications before officially starting shooting. Here, I will tell you a few of the leading actors in this film below:

Female lead: (1) Li Minghui, (2) Hu Ping, (3) Huang Naishuang. Male lead: (1) Wang Yin, (2) Wang Naidong, (3) Qin Tong. Other male and female key roles are also people with a very high position in the film industry.

It is said that: One of the female leads in "Woman" is very suitable for Li Minghui's personality, so Shi Dongshan thought of many ways to invite Li Minghui, and Li Minghui was also very willing. Of course, with the consent of both parties, the female lead of "Woman" is no problem. In this way, you can always know that the opening date of "Woman" is not far away.

Film Novel

Broadway Thru a Keyhole (4)

— Xinzhi

"Those are two different things," she said. Roche then asked her, "Do you know that there are only you and me here, it's already past midnight, and you're sitting on my bed now?" Joan raised her head and looked at him, she said, "But I believe you." Roche smiled helplessly. He took one of her hands and touched it very kindly. He said, "Joan, you're right. You can believe me. I'm going to send you home right away. You've lost your beauty sleep, go and make it up." As he said this, he really sent Joan Huilan back.

The next day, Roche ran to the business office of the Calais nightclub. He said to the old boss lady of the nightclub, Tex, "How about letting me have this place for 20,000 yuan?" Tex sat casually in a large chair, took a cigarette, put it in a very long ivory cigarette holder, and slowly said, "What can or cannot be done, just let you have it." Roche then ordered Chuck to find Max, the director of the dance. After a while, Chuck and Max came. Roche asked him, "Isn't Joan Huilan dancing pretty well?" The dance director was a little scared when he saw Roche and couldn't speak for a while. Roche said to Max again, "You can adjust the program and find a way to get Joan Huilan to be a leading role." Max threw his hand away and said to Roche, "Mr. Roche, you're joking. Do you want to see a miracle? What you're asking for is simply impossible." The thief leader restrained his anger and said, "Max, I'm afraid you misunderstood. I don't have any requests for you. If I tell you to do this, just do it." Max looked very embarrassed. But he had no way to disobey the order of this new boss.

Max worked hard to coach this newly born singing and dancing star for a few days. On the night of the premiere of the new show, Joan Huilan was in her dressing room. Her sister, Yiseier, and Chuck's girlfriend, Sybil, were also there. Yiseier said to Joan: Everyone outside will definitely be surprised, how come there is such a new character in the Calais nightclub, and she has become a pillar of the stage as soon as she comes. Everyone will also think that someone must have bribed the Calais nightclub. Why bribe? Of course, it cannot escape a universal law, that is, the command of love." Joan said, "I still don't understand what he means." After a while, a film newspaper was sent in. Joan opened it and saw the words: "Joan, take care. Roche." Her hand trembled. She said, "The time has come, I must do well!"

Joan went on stage. Roche watched silently on stage. He looked at Joan, and then at the faces of the guests sitting at the tables below the stage.

He knew Joan was very good. When the performance was nearing its climax, everyone's emotions became tense as well. Then there was a burst of crazy shouting and applause. After the play was over, Roche ran to Joan's dressing room. Joan was then lying on her sister Yisai'er's shoulders, crying and laughing, shouting, "Oh, I'm so happy, they all like me so much!" She said it over and over again. From then on, Roche did not miss a night at the Calais nightclub, and he did not miss buying flowers to send to the new lead in the nightclub. (To be continued)
